		(loadstring(game:HttpGet("https://raw.githubusercontent.com/duongquangtungnam/Scripts/refs/heads/main/NotifyBloxFruit.lua")))();

end);

end;

	local o = (plr.PlayerGui:WaitForChild("Main")):WaitForChild("Loading") and game:IsLoaded();
	wait();
until o;

local r = { RFJobsRemoteFunction = replicated.Modules.Net["RF/JobsRemoteFunction"], RFCraft = ((replicated:WaitForChild("Modules")):WaitForChild("Net")):WaitForChild("RF/Craft") };
EquipWeapon = function(o)
		if not o then
			return;
		end;
		if plr.Backpack:FindFirstChild(o) then
			plr.Character.Humanoid:EquipTool(plr.Backpack:FindFirstChild(o));
		end;
	end;
weaponSc = function(o)
		for F, J in pairs(plr.Backpack:GetChildren()) do
			if J:IsA("Tool") then
				if J.ToolTip == o then
					EquipWeapon(J.Name);
				end;
			end;
		end;
	end;
local A = {};
A.__index = A;
A.Alive = function(o)
		if not o then
			return;
		end;
		local F = o:FindFirstChild("Humanoid");
		return F and F.Health > 0;
	end;
A.Pos = function(o, F)
		return (Root.Position - mode.Position).Magnitude <= F;
	end;
A.Dist = function(o, F)
		return (Root.Position - (o:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")).Position).Magnitude <= F;
	end;
A.DistH = function(o, F)
		return (Root.Position - (o:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")).Position).Magnitude > F;
	end;
A.Kill = function(o, F)
		if o and F then
			if not o:GetAttribute("Locked") then
				o:SetAttribute("Locked", o.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame);
			end;
			PosMon = (o:GetAttribute("Locked")).Position;
			BringEnemy();
			EquipWeapon(_G.SelectWeapon);
			local F = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Tool");
			local J = F.ToolTip;
			if J == "Blox Fruit" then
				_tp((o.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 10, 0)) * CFrame.Angles(0, math.rad(90), 0));
			else
				_tp((o.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 30, 0)) * CFrame.Angles(0, math.rad(180), 0));
			end;
			if RandomCFrame then
				wait(.5);
				_tp(o.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 30, 25));
				wait(.5);
				_tp(o.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(25, 30, 0));
				wait(.5);
				_tp(o.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(-25, 30, 0));
				wait(.5);
				_tp(o.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 30, 25));
				wait(.5);
				_tp(o.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(-25, 30, 0));
			end;
		end;
	end;
A.Kill2 = function(o, F)
		if o and F then
			if not o:GetAttribute("Locked") then
				o:SetAttribute("Locked", o.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame);
			end;
			PosMon = (o:GetAttribute("Locked")).Position;

			else
				_tp((o.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 30, 8)) * CFrame.Angles(0, math.rad(180), 0));
			end;
			if RandomCFrame then
				wait(.1);
				_tp(o.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 30, 25));
				wait(.1);
				_tp(o.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(25, 30, 0));
				wait(.1);
				_tp(o.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(-25, 30, 0));
				wait(.1);
				_tp(o.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 30, 25));
				wait(.1);
				_tp(o.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(-25, 30, 0));
			end;
		end;
	end;
A.KillSea = function(o, F)
		if o and F then
			if not o:GetAttribute("Locked") then
				o:SetAttribute("Locked", o.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame);
			end;
			PosMon = (o:GetAttribute("Locked")).Position;
			BringEnemy();

				_tp((o.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 10, 0)) * CFrame.Angles(0, math.rad(90), 0));
			else
				notween(o.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 50, 8));
				wait(.85);
				notween(o.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 400, 0));
				wait(1);
			end;
		end;
	end;
A.Sword = function(o, F)
		if o and F then
			if not o:GetAttribute("Locked") then
				o:SetAttribute("Locked", o.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame);
			end;
			PosMon = (o:GetAttribute("Locked")).Position;
			BringEnemy();
			weaponSc("Sword");
			_tp(o.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 30, 0));
			if RandomCFrame then
				wait(.1);
				_tp(o.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 30, 25));
				wait(.1);
				_tp(o.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(25, 30, 0));
				wait(.1);
				_tp(o.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(-25, 30, 0));
				wait(.1);
				_tp(o.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 30, 25));
				wait(.1);
				_tp(o.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(-25, 30, 0));
			end;
		end;
	end;
A.Mas = function(o, F)
		if o and F then
			if not o:GetAttribute("Locked") then
				o:SetAttribute("Locked", o.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame);
			end;
			PosMon = (o:GetAttribute("Locked")).Position;
			BringEnemy();
			if o.Humanoid.Health <= HealthM then
				_tp(o.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 20, 0));
				Useskills("Blox Fruit", "Z");
				Useskills("Blox Fruit", "X");
				Useskills("Blox Fruit", "C");
			else
				weaponSc("Melee");
				_tp(o.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 30, 0));
			end;
		end;
	end;
A.Masgun = function(o, F)
		if o and F then
			if not o:GetAttribute("Locked") then
				o:SetAttribute("Locked", o.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame);
			end;
			PosMon = (o:GetAttribute("Locked")).Position;
			BringEnemy();
			if o.Humanoid.Health <= HealthM then
				_tp(o.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 35, 8));
				Useskills("Gun", "Z");
				Useskills("Gun", "X");
			else
				weaponSc("Melee");
				_tp(o.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 30, 0));
			end;
		end;
	end;
statsSetings = function(o, F)
		if o == "Melee" then
			if plr.Data.Points.Value ~= 0 then
				replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("AddPoint", "Melee", F);
			end;
		elseif o == "Defense" then
			if plr.Data.Points.Value ~= 0 then
				replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("AddPoint", "Defense", F);
			end;
		elseif o == "Sword" then
			if plr.Data.Points.Value ~= 0 then
				replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("AddPoint", "Sword", F);
			end;
		elseif o == "Gun" then
			if plr.Data.Points.Value ~= 0 then
				replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("AddPoint", "Gun", F);
			end;
		elseif o == "Devil" then
			if plr.Data.Points.Value ~= 0 then
				replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("AddPoint", "Demon Fruit", F);
			end;
		end;
	end;
BringEnemy = function(o)
		if not _B then
			return;
		end;
		if not o then
			local F = plr.Character and plr.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart");
			if not F then
				return;
			end;
			local J = math.huge;
			for D, G in ipairs(workspace.Enemies:GetChildren()) do
				local m = G:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid");
				local X = G:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart");
				if m and (X and m.Health > 0) then
					local D = (X.Position - F.Position).Magnitude;
					if D < J then
						J = D;
						o = G;
					end;
				end;
			end;
			if not o then
				return;
			end;
		end;
		local F = false;
		local function J(o)
			local F = o:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid");
			local J = o:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart");
			return F and (J and F.Health > 0), J, F;
		end;
		local function D(o)
			if isnetworkowner then
				return isnetworkowner(o);
			end;
			return o.ReceiveAge == 0 and (not o.Anchored and o.Velocity.Magnitude > 0);
		end;
		pcall(function()
			if sethiddenproperty then
				sethiddenproperty(plr, "SimulationRadius", math.huge);
			end;
			local G = o.HumanoidRootPart.Position;
			for m, X in ipairs(workspace.Enemies:GetChildren()) do
				if X ~= o then
					local m, V, j = J(X);
					if m and X.Name == o.Name then
						local o = (V.Position - G).Magnitude;
						if o <= 3000 then
							local J = V:FindFirstChild("BodyVelocity");
							if not J then
								J = Instance.new("BodyVelocity");
								J.Name = "BodyVelocity";
								J.MaxForce = Vector3.new(1000000000.0, 1000000000.0, 1000000000.0);
								J.Velocity = Vector3.zero;
								J.Parent = V;
							end;
							if o <= 10 then
								F = true;
							end;
							if not F and D(V) then
								V.CFrame = CFrame.new(G);
							end;
							V.CanCollide = false;
							j.WalkSpeed = 0;
							j.JumpPower = 0;
						end;
					end;
				end;
			end;
			if o and o:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
				o.HumanoidRootPart.CanCollide = false;
				o.Humanoid.WalkSpeed = 0;
				o.Humanoid.JumpPower = 0;
			end;
		end);
	end;
Useskills = function(o, F)
		if o == "Melee" then
			weaponSc("Melee");
			if F == "Z" then
				vim1:SendKeyEvent(true, "Z", false, game);
				vim1:SendKeyEvent(false, "Z", false, game);
			elseif F == "X" then
				vim1:SendKeyEvent(true, "X", false, game);
				vim1:SendKeyEvent(false, "X", false, game);
			elseif F == "C" then
				vim1:SendKeyEvent(true, "C", false, game);
				vim1:SendKeyEvent(false, "C", false, game);
			end;
		elseif o == "Sword" then
			weaponSc("Sword");
			if F == "Z" then
				vim1:SendKeyEvent(true, "Z", false, game);
				vim1:SendKeyEvent(false, "Z", false, game);
			elseif F == "X" then
				vim1:SendKeyEvent(true, "X", false, game);
				vim1:SendKeyEvent(false, "X", false, game);
			end;
		elseif o == "Blox Fruit" then
			weaponSc("Blox Fruit");
			if F == "Z" then
				vim1:SendKeyEvent(true, "Z", false, game);
				vim1:SendKeyEvent(false, "Z", false, game);
			elseif F == "X" then
				vim1:SendKeyEvent(true, "X", false, game);
				vim1:SendKeyEvent(false, "X", false, game);
			elseif F == "C" then
				vim1:SendKeyEvent(true, "C", false, game);
				vim1:SendKeyEvent(false, "C", false, game);
			elseif F == "V" then
				vim1:SendKeyEvent(true, "V", false, game);
				vim1:SendKeyEvent(false, "V", false, game);
			end;
		elseif o == "Gun" then
			weaponSc("Gun");
			if F == "Z" then
				vim1:SendKeyEvent(true, "Z", false, game);
				vim1:SendKeyEvent(false, "Z", false, game);
			elseif F == "X" then
				vim1:SendKeyEvent(true, "X", false, game);
				vim1:SendKeyEvent(false, "X", false, game);
			end;
		end;
		if o == "nil" and F == "Y" then
			vim1:SendKeyEvent(true, "Y", false, game);
			vim1:SendKeyEvent(false, "Y", false, game);
		end;
	end;
local g = getrawmetatable(game);
local l = g.__namecall;
setreadonly(g, false);
g.__namecall = newcclosure(function(...)
		local o = getnamecallmethod();
		local F = { ... };
		if tostring(o) == "FireServer" then
			if tostring(F[1]) == "RemoteEvent" then
				if tostring(F[2]) ~= "true" and tostring(F[2]) ~= "false" then
					if _G.FarmMastery_G and not SoulGuitar or _G.FarmMastery_Dev or _G.FarmBlazeEM or _G.Prehis_Skills or _G.SeaBeast1 or _G.FishBoat or _G.PGB or _G.Leviathan1 or _G.Complete_Trials or _G.AimMethod and ABmethod == "Aim Player" or _G.AimMethod and ABmethod == "Nearest Aim" then
						F[2] = MousePos;
						return l(unpack(F));
					end;
				end;
			end;
		end;
		return l(...);
	end);
GetConnectionEnemies = function(o)
		for F, J in pairs(replicated:GetChildren()) do
			if J:IsA("Model") and ((typeof(o) == "table" and table.find(o, J.Name) or J.Name == o) and (J:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") and J.Humanoid.Health > 0)) then
				return J;
			end;
		end;
		for F, J in next, game.Workspace.Enemies:GetChildren() do
			if J:IsA("Model") and ((typeof(o) == "table" and table.find(o, J.Name) or J.Name == o) and (J:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") and J.Humanoid.Health > 0)) then
				return J;
			end;
		end;
	end;
LowCpu = function()
		local o = true;
		local F = game;
		local J = F.Workspace;
		local D = F.Lighting;
		local G = J.Terrain;
		G.WaterWaveSize = 0;
		G.WaterWaveSpeed = 0;
		G.WaterReflectance = 0;
		G.WaterTransparency = 0;
		D.GlobalShadows = false;
		D.FogEnd = 9000000000.0;
		D.Brightness = 0;
		(settings()).Rendering.QualityLevel = "Level01";
		for F, J in pairs(F:GetDescendants()) do
			if J:IsA("Part") or J:IsA("Union") or J:IsA("CornerWedgePart") or J:IsA("TrussPart") then
				J.Material = "Plastic";
				J.Reflectance = 0;
			elseif J:IsA("Decal") or J:IsA("Texture") and o then
				J.Transparency = 1;
			elseif J:IsA("ParticleEmitter") or J:IsA("Trail") then
				J.Lifetime = NumberRange.new(0);
			elseif J:IsA("Explosion") then
				J.BlastPressure = 1;
				J.BlastRadius = 1;
			elseif J:IsA("Fire") or J:IsA("SpotLight") or J:IsA("Smoke") or J:IsA("Sparkles") then
				J.Enabled = false;
			elseif J:IsA("MeshPart") then
				J.Material = "Plastic";
				J.Reflectance = 0;
				J.TextureID = 10385902758728957;
			end;
		end;
		for o, F in pairs(D:GetChildren()) do
			if F:IsA("BlurEffect") or F:IsA("SunRaysEffect") or F:IsA("ColorCorrectionEffect") or F:IsA("BloomEffect") or F:IsA("DepthOfFieldEffect") then
				F.Enabled = false;
			end;
		end;
	end;
CheckF = function()
		if GetBP("Dragon-Dragon") or GetBP("Gas-Gas") or GetBP("Yeti-Yeti") or GetBP("Kitsune-Kitsune") or GetBP("T-Rex-T-Rex") then
			return true;
		end;
	end;
CheckBoat = function()

					plr.PlayerGui.Main.Dialogue.Visible = false;
				end;

				(plr.Character:FindFirstChild(F.Name)).EatRemote:InvokeServer("Drop");
			end;
		end;

			if string.find(F.Name, "Fruit") then
				EquipWeapon(F.Name);
				wait(.1);

				end;

				(plr.Character:FindFirstChild(F.Name)).EatRemote:InvokeServer("Drop");

getInfinity_Ability = function(o, F)
		if not Root then
			return;
		end;
		if o == "Soru" and F then
			for o, J in next, getgc() do
				if plr.Character.Soru then
					if typeof(J) == "function" and (getfenv(J)).script == plr.Character.Soru then
						for o, J in next, getupvalues(J) do
							if typeof(J) == "table" then
								repeat
									wait(Sec);
									J.LastUse = 0;
								until not F or plr.Character.Humanoid.Health <= 0;
							end;
						end;
					end;
				end;
			end;
		elseif o == "Energy" and F then
			plr.Character.Energy.Changed:connect(function()
				if F then
					plr.Character.Energy.Value = Energy;
				end;
			end);
		elseif o == "Observation" and F then
			local o = plr.VisionRadius;
			o.Value = math.huge;
		end;
	end;
Hop = function()
		pcall(function()
			for o = math.random(1, math.random(40, 75)), 100, 1 do
				local F = replicated.__ServerBrowser:InvokeServer(o);
				for o, F in next, F do
					if tonumber(F.Count) < 12 then
						TeleportService:TeleportToPlaceInstance(game.PlaceId, o);
					end;
				end;
			end;
		end);
	end;
local Z = Instance.new("Part", workspace);
Z.Size = Vector3.new(1, 1, 1);
Z.Name = "Rip_Indra";
Z.Anchored = true;
Z.CanCollide = false;

task.spawn(function()
	while task.wait() do
		if Z and Z.Parent == workspace then
			if shouldTween then
				(getgenv()).OnFarm = true;
			else
				(getgenv()).OnFarm = false;
			end;
		else
			(getgenv()).OnFarm = false;
		end;
	end;
end);
task.spawn(function()
	local o = game.Players.LocalPlayer;
	repeat
		task.wait();
	until o.Character and o.Character.PrimaryPart;
	Z.CFrame = o.Character.PrimaryPart.CFrame;
	while task.wait() do
		pcall(function()
			if (getgenv()).OnFarm then
				if Z and Z.Parent == workspace then
					local F = o.Character and o.Character.PrimaryPart;
					if F and (F.Position - Z.Position).Magnitude <= 200 then
						F.CFrame = Z.CFrame;
					else
						Z.CFrame = F.CFrame;
					end;
				end;
				local F = o.Character;
				if F then
					for o, F in pairs(F:GetChildren()) do
						if F:IsA("BasePart") then
							F.CanCollide = false;
						end;
					end;
				end;
			else
				local F = o.Character;
				if F then
					for o, F in pairs(F:GetChildren()) do
						if F:IsA("BasePart") then
							F.CanCollide = true;
						end;
					end;
				end;
			end;
		end);
	end;
end);
local W = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage");
local s = game:GetService("TweenService");
local S = game:GetService("RunService");
local N = game:GetService("Players");
local i = N.LocalPlayer;
sea1 = game.PlaceId == 2753915549 or game.PlaceId == 85211729168715;
sea2 = game.PlaceId == 4442272183 or game.PlaceId == 79091703265657;
sea3 = game.PlaceId == 7449423635 or game.PlaceId == 100117331123089;
local q = {
		["Tween Speed"] = 350,
		["Bypass Teleport"] = true,
		["Up Y"] = false,
		["Up Y When Low Health"] = false,
		["Same Y"] = false,
	};
local U = CFrame.new(10641.0918, -1953.92981, 9825.07031, -0.652825892, -9.2805891e-008, -0.757508039, -2.73638356e-008, 1, -9.89323823e-008, .757508039, -4.38572947e-008, -0.652825892);
local P = CFrame.new(-16271.126, 25.5847301, 1371.98755, .999396622, -5.78875188e-008, -0.0347310975, 5.52972779e-008, 1, -8.7544322e-008, .034731105, 8.28877091e-008, .999396741);
function Convert_CFrame(o)
	if not o then
		return;
	end;
	if typeof(o) == "Vector3" then
		return CFrame.new(o);
	elseif typeof(o) == "CFrame" then
		return o;
	elseif typeof(o) == "Model" then
		return o:GetPivot();
	elseif o.CFrame then
		return o.CFrame;
	end;
	return nil;
end;
function GetDistance(o, F, J)
	if o == nil then
		return 9000000000.0;
	end;
	local D = i.Character;
	if not D then
		return 9000000000.0;
	end;
	local G = D:FindFirstChild("Humanoid");
	if not G or G.Health <= 0 then
		return 9000000000.0;
	end;
	if F == nil then
		F = D:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart");
		if not F then
			return 9000000000.0;
		end;
	end;
	local m = Convert_CFrame(o);
	local X = Convert_CFrame(F);
	if J then
		return (Vector3.new(m.X, 0, m.Z) - Vector3.new(X.X, 0, X.Z)).Magnitude;
	else
		return (m.Position - X.Position).Magnitude;
	end;
end;
function InArea(o)
	local F = workspace:FindFirstChild("_WorldOrigin");
	if not F then
		return { Name = "" };
	end;
	local J = Convert_CFrame(o);
	for o, F in next, F.Locations:GetChildren() do
		if F:FindFirstChild("Mesh") and (J.Position - F.Position).Magnitude <= F.Mesh.Scale.X then
			return F;
		end;
	end;
	return { Name = "" };
end;
function GetSpawnPoint(o)
	local F = workspace:FindFirstChild("_WorldOrigin") and (workspace._WorldOrigin:FindFirstChild("PlayerSpawns") and workspace._WorldOrigin.PlayerSpawns:FindFirstChild("Pirates"));
	if not F then
		return;
	end;
	for F, J in next, F:GetChildren() do
		if J:FindFirstChild("Part") and (J.Part.Position - o.Position).Magnitude <= 2500 then
			return J;
		end;
	end;
end;
function CheckLegendaryItems()
	local function o(o)
		for F, J in next, i.Backpack:GetChildren() do
			if J:IsA("Tool") and (J.Name == o or string.find(J.Name, o)) then
				return J;
			end;
		end;
		for F, J in next, i.Character:GetChildren() do
			if J:IsA("Tool") and (J.Name == o or string.find(J.Name, o)) then
				return J;
			end;
		end;
	end;
	if o("God\'s Chalice") or o("Fist of Darkness") or o("Sweet Chalice") or o("Hallow Essence") or o("Flower1") then
		return true;
	end;
	return false;
end;
function WaitForHumanoid()
	local o = i.Character;
	if not o then
		return nil;
	end;
	local F = o:FindFirstChild("Humanoid");
	if F then
		return F;
	end;
	local J = tick() + 5;
	while tick() < J do
		F = o:FindFirstChild("Humanoid");
		if F then
			return F;
		end;
		task.wait(.1);
	end;
	return nil;
end;
function checkinventory(o)
	if o then
		for F, J in pairs(W.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("getInventory")) do
			if J.Name == o then
				return true;
			end;
		end;
	end;
	return false;
end;
function getdis(o, F)
	F = F or i.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame;
	local J = CFrame.new(o.X, F.Y, o.Z);
	local D = CFrame.new(F.X, F.Y, F.Z);
	return (J.Position - D.Position).Magnitude;
end;
function CanBypassTeleport(o)
	local F = (InArea(o)).Name;
	if F == "" then
		return false;
	end;
	if not q["Bypass Teleport"] or F:find("Dimension") or F:find("Submerged") or F == "Sealed Cavern" or (F:lower()):find("under") or CheckLegendaryItems() then
		return false;
	end;
	if i.Data and (i.Data.LastSpawnPoint and i.Data.LastSpawnPoint.Value == "SubmergedIsland") then
		return false;
	end;
	if GetDistance(o.Position) <= 3500 then
		return false;
	end;
	return true;
end;
function GetBypassCFrame(o)
	local F = math.huge;
	local J;
	local D = workspace._WorldOrigin.PlayerSpawns.Pirates:GetChildren();
	local G = i.Character and i.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart");
	if not G then
		return nil;
	end;
	for D, m in next, D do
		if m:FindFirstChild("Part") then
			if (o.Position - G.Position).Magnitude >= 3000 and (GetSpawnPoint(m.Part) ~= GetSpawnPoint(G) and ((m.Part.Position - G.Position).Magnitude <= 10000 and (m.Part.Position - o.Position).Magnitude <= F)) then
				F = (m.Part.Position - o.Position).Magnitude;
				J = m;
			end;
		end;
	end;
	return J;
end;
function BypassTP(o)
	local F = i.Character;
	if not F then
		return;
	end;
	local J = WaitForHumanoid();
	if not J or J.Health <= 0 then
		return;
	end;
	if CanBypassTeleport(o) and GetBypassCFrame(o) then
		local D = GetBypassCFrame(o);
		if D and D:FindFirstChild("Part") then
			F.LastSpawnPoint.Disabled = true;
			W.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("SetLastSpawnPoint", D.Name);
			W.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("SetSpawnPoint");
			F:PivotTo(D.Part.CFrame);
			J:ChangeState(15);
			repeat
				task.wait();
			until i.Character and (WaitForHumanoid() and (WaitForHumanoid()).Health > 0);
		end;
	end;
end;
function totopofgreattree()
	if getdis(CFrame.new(28310.0234, 14895.1123, 109.456741)) > 1500 then
		W.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("requestEntrance", Vector3.new(28310.0234, 14895.1123, 109.456741));
		wait(.3);
	end;
	local o = CFrame.new(28607.5352, 14896.5449, 106.011726);
	_tp(o);
	repeat
		wait();
	until getdis(o) <= 5;
	wait(.5);
	for o = 1, 4, 1 do
		W.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("RaceV4Progress", "TeleportBack");
	end;
end;
function requestentrance(o)
	local F = {};
	local J = o;
	if typeof(o) == "CFrame" then
		J = o.Position;
	end;
	if sea1 then
		F = {
				Sky3 = Vector3.new(-7894, 5547, -380),
				Sky3Exit = Vector3.new(-4607, 874, -1667),
				UnderWater = Vector3.new(61163, 11, 1819),
				["Underwater City"] = Vector3.new(61165.19140625, .18704631924629, 1897.3791503906),
				["Pirate Village"] = Vector3.new(-1242.4625244141, 4.7870597839355, 3901.2829589844),
				UnderwaterExit = Vector3.new(4050, -1, -1814),
			};
	elseif sea2 then
		F = {
				["Swan Mansion"] = Vector3.new(-390, 332, 673),
				["Swan Room"] = Vector3.new(2285, 15, 905),
				["Cursed Ship"] = Vector3.new(923, 126, 32852),
				["Zombie Island"] = Vector3.new(-6509, 83, -133),
			};
	else
		F = {
				["Hydra Island"] = Vector3.new(5657.8862304688, 1013.0790405273, -335.49963378906),
				Mansion = Vector3.new(-12462, 375, -7552),
				Castle = Vector3.new(-5036, 315, -3179),
				["Temple of Time"] = Vector3.new(28286, 14897, 103),
				["Greate Tree"] = Vector3.new(3024.1709, 2280.69434, -7325.12793),
			};
		if not checkinventory("Valkyrie Helm") then
			return;
		end;
	end;
	local D, G = nil, math.huge;
	for o, F in pairs(F) do
		local m = typeof(F) == "Vector3" and (F - J).Magnitude or (F.Position - J).Magnitude;
		if m < G then
			G = m;
			D = F;
		end;
	end;
	if D and (G and G < getdis(o)) then
		pcall(function()
			if _G.TweenCache then
				_G.TweenCache:Cancel();
			end;
		end);
		if typeof(D) == "Vector3" and (D.X == 3024.1709 and (D.Y == 2280.69434 and (D.Z == -7325.12793 and W.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("RaceV4Progress", "Check") >= 2))) then
			totopofgreattree();
			wait(1);
		elseif G < getdis(o) then
			local o = typeof(D) == "Vector3" and D or D.Position;
			W.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("requestEntrance", o);
			wait(1);
		end;
	end;
end;
_tp = function(o)
		local F;
		if typeof(o) == "Vector3" then
			F = CFrame.new(o);
		elseif typeof(o) == "CFrame" then
			F = o;
		else
			F = o and o.CFrame;
		end;
		if not F then
			return;
		end;
		local J = plr.Character;
		if not J or not J:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
			return;
		end;
		local D = J.HumanoidRootPart;
		pcall(function()
			if CanBypassTeleport(F) then
				BypassTP(F);
				task.wait(.5);
			end;
		end);
		pcall(function()
			requestentrance(o);
		end);
		if sea3 and getdis(F.Position, U.Position) < 2000 then
			local o = plr.Character.HumanoidRootPart;
			if math.abs(U.Position.Y - o.CFrame.Y) > 1000 then
				repeat
					task.wait();
					old_tp(P);
					if getdis(P) < 10 then
						local o = W.Modules.Net;
						o["RF/SubmarineWorkerSpeak"]:InvokeServer("AskKilledTikiBoss");
						task.wait(.5);
						o["RF/SubmarineWorkerSpeak"]:InvokeServer("TravelToSubmergedIsland");
					end;
				until getdis(F.Position) < 2000;
				task.wait(.6);
				pcall(function()
					if o:FindFirstChild("BodyClip") then
						o.BodyClip:Destroy();
					end;
				end);
			end;
		end;
		local G = (F.Position - D.Position).Magnitude;
		local m = TweenInfo.new(G / 300, Enum.EasingStyle.Linear);
		local X = (game:GetService("TweenService")):Create(Z, m, { CFrame = F });
		if plr.Character.Humanoid.Sit == true then
			Z.CFrame = CFrame.new(Z.Position.X, F.Y, Z.Position.Z);
		end;
		X:Play();
		task.spawn(function()
			while X.PlaybackState == Enum.PlaybackState.Playing do
				if not shouldTween then
					X:Cancel();
					break;
				end;
				task.wait(.1);
			end;
		end);
		return X;
	end;
old_tp = function(o)
		local F = plr.Character;
		if F and F:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
			F.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = o;
		end;
	end;
TeleportToTarget = function(o)
		if (o.Position - plr.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude > 1000 then
			_tp(o);
		else
			_tp(o);
		end;
	end;
notween = function(o)
		plr.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = o;
	end;
function BTP(o)
	local F = game.Players.LocalPlayer;
	local J = F.Character.HumanoidRootPart;
	local D = F.Character.Humanoid;
	local G = F.PlayerGui.Main;
	local m = o.Position;
	local X = J.Position;
	repeat
		D.Health = 0;
		J.CFrame = o;
		G.Quest.Visible = false;
		if (J.Position - X).Magnitude > 1 then
			X = J.Position;
			J.CFrame = o;
		end;
		task.wait(.5);
	until (o.Position - J.Position).Magnitude <= 2000;
end;
spawn(function()
	while task.wait() do
		pcall(function()
			if _G.SailBoat_Hydra or _G.WardenBoss or _G.AutoFactory or _G.HighestMirage or _G.HCM or _G.PGB or _G.Leviathan1 or _G.UPGDrago or _G.Complete_Trials or _G.TpDrago_Prehis or _G.BuyDrago or _G.AutoFireFlowers or _G.DT_Uzoth or _G.AutoBerry or _G.Prefully or _G.Prehis_Find or _G.Prehis_Skills or _G.Prehis_DB or _G.Prehis_DE or _G.FarmBlazeEM or _G.Dojoo or _G.CollectPresent or _G.AutoLawKak or _G.TpLab or _G.AutoPhoenixF or _G.AutoFarmChest or _G.AutoHytHallow or _G.LongsWord or _G.BlackSpikey or _G.AutoHolyTorch or _G.TrainDrago or _G.AutoSaber or _G.FarmMastery_Dev or _G.AutoTPAndCollect or _G.MasterAutoLevel or _G.MasterAutoCandy or _G.TPFloor1 or _G.TPFloor2 or _G.TPFloor3 or _G.TPFloor4 then

				if not plr.Character.HumanoidRootPart:FindFirstChild("BodyClip") then
					local o = Instance.new("BodyVelocity");
					o.Name = "BodyClip";
					o.Parent = plr.Character.HumanoidRootPart;
					o.MaxForce = Vector3.new(100000, 100000, 100000);
					o.Velocity = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0);
				end;
				if not plr.Character:FindFirstChild("highlight") then
					local o = Instance.new("Highlight");
					o.Name = "highlight";
					o.Enabled = true;
					o.FillColor = Color3.fromRGB(0, 255, 254);
					o.OutlineColor = Color3.fromRGB(0, 255, 254);
					o.FillTransparency = .5;
					o.OutlineTransparency = .2;
					o.Parent = plr.Character;
				end;
				for o, F in pairs(plr.Character:GetDescendants()) do
					if F:IsA("BasePart") then
						F.CanCollide = false;
					end;
				end;
			else
				shouldTween = false;
				if plr.Character.HumanoidRootPart:FindFirstChild("BodyClip") then
					(plr.Character.HumanoidRootPart:FindFirstChild("BodyClip")):Destroy();
				end;
				if plr.Character:FindFirstChild("highlight") then
					(plr.Character:FindFirstChild("highlight")):Destroy();
				end;
			end;
		end);
	end;

QuestBeta = function()
		local o = QuestB();
		return {
			[0] = _G.FindBoss,
			[1] = bMon,
			[2] = Qdata,
			[3] = Qname,

local C = require((game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")):WaitForChild("Quests"));
local t = require((game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")):WaitForChild("GuideModule"));
local h = {
		"MarineQuest",
		"BartiloQuest",
		"CitizenQuest",
		"Trainees",
	};
CheckSea = function(o)
		if (game.PlaceId == 2753915549 or game.PlaceId == 85211729168715) and o == 1 then
			return true;
		elseif (game.PlaceId == 4442272183 or game.PlaceId == 79091703265657) and o == 2 then
			return true;
		elseif (game.PlaceId == 7449423635 or game.PlaceId == 100117331123089) and o == 3 then
			return true;
		end;
		return false;
	end;
GetQuestPointFromNPC = function(o)
		for F, J in pairs(workspace.NPCs:GetChildren()) do
			if J.Name == o and J:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
				return J.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame;
			end;
		end;
		for F, J in pairs(replicated.NPCs:GetChildren()) do
			if J.Name == o and J:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
				return J.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame;
			end;
		end;
		return nil;
	end;
GetQuests = function()
		local o = plr.Data.Level.Value;
		local F = 0;
		local J = {};
		if o >= 700 and CheckSea(1) then
			J.Mob = "Galley Captain";
			J.NameQuest = "FountainQuest";
			J.ID = 2;
			J.LevelReq = 700;
		elseif o >= 1500 and CheckSea(2) then
			J.Mob = "Water Fighter";
			J.NameQuest = "ForgottenQuest";
			J.ID = 2;
			J.LevelReq = 1450;
		else
			for D, G in pairs(C) do
				for G, m in pairs(G) do
					local X = m.LevelReq;
					for V, j in pairs(m.Task) do
						if o >= X and (F <= X and (m.Task[V] > 1 and not table.find(h, D))) then
							F = X;
							J.Mob = V;
							J.NameQuest = D;
							J.ID = G;
							J.LevelReq = X;
						end;
					end;
				end;
			end;
		end;
		return J;
	end;
GetQuestPoint = function()
		if t and (t.Data and t.Data.LastClosestNPC) then
			return GetQuestPointFromNPC(t.Data.LastClosestNPC);
		end;
		return nil;
	end;
MaterialMon = function()
		local o = game.Players.LocalPlayer;
		local F = o.Character and o.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart");
		if not F then
			return;
		end;
		shouldRequestEntrance = function(o, J)
				local D = (F.Position - o).Magnitude;
				if D >= J then
					replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("requestEntrance", o);
				end;
			end;
		if World1 then
			if SelectMaterial == "Angel Wings" then
				MMon = {
						"Shanda",

				MPos = CFrame.new(-1145, 15, 4350);
				SP = "Default";

				MMon = { "Military Soldier", "Military Spy", "Magma Admiral" };

				SP = "Default";

				MMon = { "Fishman Warrior", "Fishman Commando", "Fishman Lord" };
				MPos = CFrame.new(61123, 19, 1569);
				SP = "Default";
				local o = Vector3.new(61163.8515625, 5.342342376709, 1819.7841796875);
				shouldRequestEntrance(o, 17000);
			end;
		elseif World2 then
			if SelectMaterial == "Leather + Scrap Metal" then

local x = I.Info:AddParagraph("Time Zone", "");
function UpdateOS()
	local o = os.date("*t");
	local F = o.hour % 24;
	local J = F < 12 and "AM" or "PM";
	local D = string.format("%02i:%02i:%02i %s", (F - 1) % 12 + 1, o.min, o.sec, J);
	local G = string.format("%02d/%02d/%04d", o.day, o.month, o.year);
	local m = game:GetService("LocalizationService");
	local X = game:GetService("Players");
	local V = X.LocalPlayer;
	local j, Y;
	if not (getgenv()).countryRegionCode then
		j, Y = pcall(function()
				return m:GetCountryRegionForPlayerAsync(V);
			end);
		if j then
			(getgenv()).countryRegionCode = Y;
		else
			(getgenv()).countryRegionCode = "Unknown";
		end;
	else
		Y = (getgenv()).countryRegionCode;
	end;
	x:SetDesc(G .. (" - " .. (D .. (" [ " .. (Y .. " ]")))));
end;
spawn(function()
	while true do
		UpdateOS();
		wait(1);
	end;
end);
local b = I.Info:AddParagraph("Game Time", "");
function UpdateGameTime()
	local o = math.floor(workspace.DistributedGameTime + .5);
	local F = math.floor(o / 3600.0) % 24;
	local J = math.floor(o / 60.0) % 60;
	local D = math.floor(o / 1.0) % 60;
	b:SetDesc(F .. (" Hour (h) " .. (J .. (" Minute (m) " .. (D .. " Second (s)")))));
end;
spawn(function()
	while true do
		UpdateGameTime();
		wait(1);
	end;
end);

local F4 = false;
local J4 = false;
local function D4()
	local o = plr.Character;
	if not o then
		return false;
	end;
	local F = o:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart");
	if not F then
		return false;
	end;
	local J = Vector3.new(11520.801757812, 0, 9829.513671875);
	local D = Vector3.new(F.Position.X, 0, F.Position.Z);
	return (D - J).Magnitude < 2000;
end;
task.spawn(function()
	while task.wait(Sec) do
		if _G.Level then
			pcall(function()
				local o = plr.Character or plr.CharacterAdded:Wait();
				local F = o:WaitForChild("HumanoidRootPart");
				if not F then
					return;
				end;
				local J = plr.Data.Level.Value;
				local D = D4();
				local G = plr.PlayerGui.Main.Quest;
				local m = G.Visible and G.Container.QuestTitle.Title.Text or "";
				if J >= 2600 and (not D and (not J4 and not F4)) then
					J4 = true;
					local o = CFrame.new(-16269.7041, 25.2288494, 1373.65955);
					local J = 0;
					repeat
						task.wait(Sec);
						_tp(o);
						J = J + 1;
					until not _G.Level or (F.Position - o.Position).Magnitude <= 8 or J > 20;
					if not _G.Level then
						J4 = false;
						return;
					end;
					task.wait(1);
					pcall(function()
						local o = { "TravelToSubmergedIsland" };
						((game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")).Modules.Net:FindFirstChild("RF/SubmarineWorkerSpeak")):InvokeServer(unpack(o));
					end);
					local D = tick();
					repeat
						task.wait(.5);
						local J = D4();
						local G = (F.Position - o.Position).Magnitude > 50;
						if J or G then
							break;
						end;
					until not _G.Level or tick() - D > 15;
					task.wait(2);
					F4 = true;
					J4 = false;
				elseif D or J < 2600 then
					F4 = true;
					J4 = false;
					local o = QuestNeta();
					if not o or not o[1] then
						task.wait(1);
						return;
					end;
					if G.Visible and not string.find(m, o[1]) then
						replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("AbandonQuest");
						task.wait(.2);
						return;
					end;
					if not G.Visible then
						local J = o[6];
						if J then
							_tp(J);
							task.wait(2);
							if (F.Position - J.Position).Magnitude <= 10 then
								pcall(function()
									replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("StartQuest", o[3], o[2]);
								end);
								task.wait(1);
							end;
						else
							pcall(function()
								replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("StartQuest", o[3], o[2]);
							end);
							task.wait(1);
						end;
						return;
					end;
					local J = o[1];
					local D = false;
					for o, F in pairs(workspace.Enemies:GetChildren()) do
						if F.Name == J and A.Alive(F) then
							D = true;
							repeat
								task.wait(Sec);
								_tp(F.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 20, 0));
								A.Kill(F, _G.Level);
								if not G.Visible then
									break;
								end;
							until not _G.Level or not F.Parent or F.Humanoid.Health <= 0;
							break;
						end;
					end;
					if not D then
						for o, F in pairs(replicated:GetChildren()) do
							if F.Name == J and A.Alive(F) then
								D = true;
								_tp(F.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 20, 0));
								break;
							end;
						end;
					end;
					if not D then
						for o, F in pairs(workspace._WorldOrigin.EnemySpawns:GetChildren()) do
							if string.find(F.Name, J) then
								_tp(F.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 20, 0));
								break;
							end;
						end;
					end;
				end;
			end);
		else
			J4 = false;
			F4 = false;
		end;
	end;
end);

		Default = false,
		Callback = function(o)
			_G.AutoChestBP = o;
			if o then
				local o = (game:GetService("Players")).LocalPlayer;
				local F = false;
				local J = {};
				local D = true;
				local function G()
					if not o.Character then
						o.CharacterAdded:Wait();
					end;
					o.Character:WaitForChild("HumanoidRootPart");
					return o.Character;
				end;
				local function m()
					if D then
						D = false;
						for o, F in pairs(game:GetDescendants()) do
							if F.Name:find("Chest") and F.ClassName == "Part" then
								table.insert(J, F);
							end;
						end;
					end;
					local o = {};
					for F, J in pairs(J) do
						if J:FindFirstChild("TouchInterest") then
							table.insert(o, J);
						end;
					end;
					local F = (G()).LowerTorso;
					table.sort(o, function(o, J)
						return (F.Position - o.Position).Magnitude < (F.Position - J.Position).Magnitude;
					end);
					return o;
				end;
				local function X()
					if F then
						return;
					end;
					F = true;
					task.spawn(function()
						while _G.AutoChestBP and (o.Character and o.Character.Parent) do
							local o = m();
							if #o > 0 then
								local F = (G()).HumanoidRootPart;
								F.CFrame = o[1].CFrame;
							end;
							task.wait(.1);
						end;
						F = false;
					end);
				end;
				o.CharacterAdded:Connect(function()
					G();
					task.wait(.5);
					if _G.AutoChestBP then
						X();
					end;
				end);
				X();
			end;
		end,
	});

spawn(function()
	while wait(Sec) do
		if _G.AutoBerry then
			local o = game:GetService("CollectionService");
			local F = game:GetService("Players");
			local J = F.LocalPlayer;
			local D = o:GetTagged("BerryBush");
			local G, m = math.huge;
			for o = 1, #D, 1 do
				local F = D[o];
				for o, J in pairs(F:GetAttributes()) do
					if not BerryArray or table.find(BerryArray, J) then
						_tp(F.Parent:GetPivot());
						for o = 1, #D, 1 do
							local F = D[o];
							for o, F in pairs(F:GetChildren()) do
								if not BerryArray or table.find(BerryArray, F) then
									_tp(F.WorldPivot);
									fireproximityprompt(F.ProximityPrompt, math.huge);
								end;
							end;
						end;
					end;
				end;
			end;
		end;
	end;
end);

			local J = F.LocalPlayer;
			local D = o:GetTagged("BerryBush");
			if #D == 0 then
				local o = game:GetService("TeleportService");
				local F = {};
				local D, G = pcall(function()
						F = (game:GetService("HttpService")):JSONDecode(game:HttpGet("https://games.roblox.com/v1/games/" .. (game.PlaceId .. "/servers/Public?sortOrder=Asc&limit=100")));
					end);
				if D and F.data then
					for F, D in pairs(F.data) do
						if D.playing < D.maxPlayers and D.id ~= game.JobId then
							o:TeleportToPlaceInstance(game.PlaceId, D.id, J);
							break;
						end;
					end;
				end;
			else
				for o = 1, #D, 1 do
					local F = D[o];
					for o, J in pairs(F:GetAttributes()) do
						if not BerryArray or table.find(BerryArray, J) then
							_tp(F.Parent:GetPivot());
							for o = 1, #D, 1 do
								local F = D[o];
								for o, F in pairs(F:GetChildren()) do
									if not BerryArray or table.find(BerryArray, F.Name) then
										_tp(F.WorldPivot);
										fireproximityprompt(F.ProximityPrompt, math.huge);
									end;
								end;
							end;
						end;
					end;
				end;
			end;
		end;
	end;
end);

I.Main:AddToggle({ Name = "Auto Farm All Island", Default = false, Callback = function(o)
		_G.AutoFarmIsland = o;
	end });
task.spawn(function()
	while task.wait(.2) do
		if not _G.AutoFarmIsland then
			continue;
		end;
		if not _G.SelectIsland then
			continue;
		end;
		if not V4 then
			continue;
		end;
		local o = V4[_G.SelectIsland];
		if not o then
			continue;
		end;
		local F = o.CFrame;
		local J = o.Mobs;
		local D = {};
		for o, F in ipairs(J) do
			D[F] = true;
		end;
		local G = false;
		for o, F in pairs(workspace.Enemies:GetChildren()) do
			if D[F.Name] and (F:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") and (F:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") and F.Humanoid.Health > 0)) then
				G = true;
				repeat
					task.wait();
					_tp(F.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 10, 0));
					A.Kill(F, true);
				until not _G.AutoFarmIsland or not F.Parent or F.Humanoid.Health <= 0;
			end;
		end;
		if not G then
			_tp(F);
		end;
	end;
end);

		local F = ((game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")):FindFirstChild("Diablo") or (game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")):FindFirstChild("Deandre") or (game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")):FindFirstChild("Urban") or (game:GetService("Workspace")).Enemies:FindFirstChild("Diablo") or (game:GetService("Workspace")).Enemies:FindFirstChild("Deandre") or (game:GetService("Workspace")).Enemies:FindFirstChild("Urban")) and "\226\156\133" or "\226\157\140";
		local J = (game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")).Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("EliteHunter", "Progress");
		if F ~= o then
			Y4:SetDesc("Status: " .. (F .. (" | Killed: " .. J)));

EliteQ = I.Main:AddToggle({
		Name = "Auto Farm Elite",
		Description = "",
		Default = false,
		Callback = function(o)
			_G.FarmEliteHunt = o;
		end,
	});
spawn(function()
	while wait(1) do
		pcall(function()
			if _G.FarmEliteHunt then
				local o = plr.PlayerGui.Main.Quest;
				local F = o.Container.QuestTitle.Title.Text;
				if not o.Visible then
					local o = replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("EliteHunter");
					if o == nil or string.find(o, "Cooldown") then
						wait(10);
						return;
					end;
					task.wait(1);
				else
					local J = nil;
					for o, D in pairs({ "Diablo", "Urban", "Deandre" }) do
						if string.find(F, D) then
							J = D;
							break;
						end;
					end;
					if J then
						local F = nil;
						for o, D in pairs(replicated:GetChildren()) do
							if D.Name == J and D:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
								F = D;
								break;
							end;
						end;
						for o, D in pairs(Enemies:GetChildren()) do
							if D.Name == J and A.Alive(D) then
								F = D;
								break;
							end;
						end;
						if F and F:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
							_tp(F.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 30, 0));
							repeat
								wait();
								A.Kill(F, _G.FarmEliteHunt);
							until not _G.FarmEliteHunt or not F.Parent or F.Humanoid.Health <= 0 or not o.Visible;
						else
							wait(5);
						end;
					else
						replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("AbandonQuest");
					end;
				end;
			end;
		end);
	end;
end);
EliteH = I.Main:AddToggle({
		Name = "Auto Farm Elite + Hop",
		Description = "",
		Default = false,
		Callback = function(o)
			_G.FarmEliteH = o;
		end,
	});
local function B4()
	local o = game:GetService("HttpService");
	local F = game:GetService("TeleportService");
	local J = "https://games.roblox.com/v1/games/";
	local D = game.PlaceId;
	local G = {};
	local m = "";
	local X = false;
	repeat
		local G, V = pcall(function()
				return game:HttpGet(J .. (D .. ("/servers/Public?sortOrder=Asc&limit=100&cursor=" .. m)));
			end);
		if G and V then
			local J = o:JSONDecode(V);
			if J.data then
				for o, J in pairs(J.data) do
					if J.playing < J.maxPlayers and J.id ~= game.JobId then
						X = true;
						F:TeleportToPlaceInstance(D, J.id);
						break;
					end;
				end;
				m = J.nextPageCursor or "";
			end;
		end;
	until not m or X;
end;
spawn(function()
	while task.wait(1) do
		pcall(function()
			if _G.FarmEliteH then
				local o = plr.PlayerGui.Main.Quest;
				local F = o.Container.QuestTitle.Title.Text;
				if not o.Visible then
					local o = replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("EliteHunter");
					if o == nil or string.find(o, "Cooldown") then
						B4();
						return;
					end;
					task.wait(1);
				else
					local J = nil;
					for o, D in pairs({ "Diablo", "Urban", "Deandre" }) do
						if string.find(F, D) then
							J = D;
							break;
						end;
					end;
					if J then
						local F = nil;
						for o, D in pairs(replicated:GetChildren()) do
							if D.Name == J and D:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
								F = D;
								break;
							end;
						end;
						for o, D in pairs(workspace.Enemies:GetChildren()) do
							if D.Name == J and A.Alive(D) then
								F = D;
								break;
							end;
						end;
						if F and F:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
							_tp(F.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 30, 0));
							repeat
								wait();
								A.Kill(F, _G.FarmEliteH);
							until not _G.FarmEliteH or not F.Parent or F.Humanoid.Health <= 0 or not o.Visible;
						else
							task.wait(5);
							B4();
						end;
					else
						replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("AbandonQuest");
						task.wait(1);
						B4();
					end;
				end;
			end;
		end);
	end;
end);

spawn(function()

AuraSkin = function(o)
		local F = { [1] = { StorageName = o, Type = "AuraSkin", Context = "Equip" } };
		(((replicated:WaitForChild("Modules")):WaitForChild("Net")):WaitForChild("RF/FruitCustomizerRF")):InvokeServer(unpack(F));
	end;
VaildColor = function(o)
		if o and o.BrickColor then
			return tostring(o.BrickColor) == "Lime green";
		end;
	end;
HakiCalculate = function(o)
		local F = { ["Really red"] = "Pure Red", Oyster = "Snow White", ["Hot pink"] = "Winter Sky" };
		if o and o.BrickColor then
			return F[tostring(o.BrickColor)];
		end;
	end;
spawn(function()
	while wait(Sec) do
		if _G.AutoUnHaki then
			pcall(function()
				local o = workspace.Map["Boat Castle"]:FindFirstChild("Summoner");
				if o and o:FindFirstChild("Circle") then
					for o, F in pairs((o:FindFirstChild("Circle")):GetChildren()) do
						if F.Name == "Part" then
							local o = F:FindFirstChild("Part");
							if VaildColor(o) == false then
								AuraSkin(HakiCalculate(F));
								repeat
									wait();
									_tp(F.CFrame);
								until VaildColor(o) == true or not _G.AutoUnHaki;
							end;
						end;
					end;
				end;
			end);
		end;
	end;
end);

local function A4()
	pcall(function()
		local o = game:GetService("HttpService");
		local F = {};
		local J = game:HttpGet("https://games.roblox.com/v1/games/" .. (game.PlaceId .. "/servers/Public?sortOrder=Asc&limit=100"));
		local D = o:JSONDecode(J);
		for o, J in pairs(D.data) do
			if J.playing < J.maxPlayers then
				table.insert(F, J.id);
			end;
		end;
		if #F > 0 then
			(game:GetService("TeleportService")):TeleportToPlaceInstance(game.PlaceId, F[math.random(1, #F)], game.Players.LocalPlayer);
		end;
	end);
end;
spawn(function()
	while task.wait() do
		if _G.AutoHop_Dough then
			pcall(function()
				local o = GetConnectionEnemies("Dough King");
				if o then
					repeat
						task.wait();
						A.Kill(o, _G.AutoHop_Dough);
					until not _G.AutoHop_Dough or not o.Parent or o.Humanoid.Health <= 0;
				else
					_tp(CFrame.new(-1943.6765, 251.5095, -12337.8809));
					task.wait(2);
					local o = GetConnectionEnemies("Dough King");
					if not o and _G.AutoHop_Dough then
						A4();
					end;
				end;
			end);
		end;
	end;
end);

local Z4 = I.Main:AddParagraph("Check Status Eyes", "");
function Check_Eye()
	local o = workspace.Map.TikiOutpost.IslandModel;
	local F = {
			o.Eye1,
			o.Eye2,
			o.IslandChunks.E.Eye3,
			o.IslandChunks.E.Eye4,
		};
	local J = 0;
	for o, F in ipairs(F) do
		if F and F.Transparency ~= 1 then
			J = J + 1;
		end;
	end;
	local D = J == 4;
	return J, D;
end;
task.spawn(function()
	local o = false;
	while task.wait(1) do
		local F, J = Check_Eye();
		Z4:SetDesc("Eyes: " .. (F .. "/4"));
		if J and not o then
			o = true;
		elseif not J then
			o = false;
		end;
	end;
end);
FarmTyrant = I.Main:AddToggle({
		Name = "Auto Farm Boss TOTS",
		Description = "",
		Default = false,
		Callback = function(o)
			_G.FarmTyrant = o;
		end,
	});
spawn(function()
	while wait(Sec) do
		if _G.FarmTyrant then
			pcall(function()
				if not plr.Character then
					return;
				end;
				local o = plr.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart");
				if not o then
					return;
				end;
				local F = Vector3.new(-16268.287, 152.616, 1390.773);
				if (o.Position - F).Magnitude > 5 then
					_tp(CFrame.new(F));
					repeat
						wait();
					until not _G.FarmTyrant or plr.Character and (plr.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") and (plr.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position - F).Magnitude <= 5);
				end;
				local J = workspace.Enemies:FindFirstChild("Tyrant of the Skies");
				if J and (J:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") and J.Humanoid.Health > 0) then
					repeat
						if not _G.FarmTyrant then
							break;
						end;
						if A and A.Kill then
							A.Kill(J, _G.FarmTyrant);
						end;
						wait();
					until not _G.FarmTyrant or not J.Parent or J.Humanoid.Health <= 0;
					return;
				end;
				local D = {
						"Serpent Hunter",
						"Skull Slayer",
						"Isle Champion",
						"Sun-kissed Warrior",
					};
				for F, J in ipairs(D) do
					if not _G.FarmTyrant then
						break;
					end;
					for F, D in pairs(workspace.Enemies:GetChildren()) do
						if not _G.FarmTyrant then
							break;
						end;
						if D and (D.Name == J and (D:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") and (D:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") and D.Humanoid.Health > 0))) then
							if (o.Position - D.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude > 5000 then
								_tp(D.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 30, 0));
								local F = tick();
								repeat
									wait();
									o = plr.Character and plr.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart");
								until not _G.FarmTyrant or not o or (o.Position - D.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude <= 6 or tick() - F > 8;
							end;
							repeat
								if not _G.FarmTyrant then
									break;
								end;
								if A and A.Kill then
									A.Kill(D, _G.FarmTyrant);
								end;
								wait();
							until not _G.FarmTyrant or not D.Parent or D.Humanoid.Health <= 0;
						end;
					end;
				end;
			end);
		end;
	end;
end);
FarmPhaBinh = I.Main:AddToggle({
		Name = "Auto Summon Boss",
		Description = "",
		Default = false,
		Callback = function(o)
			_G.FarmPhaBinh = o;
		end,
	});
local function v4(o)
	local F = game:GetService("VirtualInputManager");
	F:SendKeyEvent(true, o, false, game);
	wait(.05);
	F:SendKeyEvent(false, o, false, game);
end;
local function W4(o)
	local F = plr.Character;
	local J = plr.Backpack;
	if not (F and (F:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") and F.Humanoid.Health > 0)) then
		return;
	end;
	for D, G in pairs(J:GetChildren()) do
		if G:IsA("Tool") and G.ToolTip == o then
			G.Parent = F;
			wait(.12);
			for o, F in ipairs({
				"Z",
				"X",
				"C",
				"V",
				"F",
			}) do
				if not _G.FarmPhaBinh then
					break;
				end;
				pcall(function()
					v4(F);
				end);
				wait(.12);
			end;
			G.Parent = J;
			break;
		end;
	end;
end;

		if _G.FarmPhaBinh then
			pcall(function()
				if not (plr and (plr.Character and (plr.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") and (plr.Character:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") and plr.Character.Humanoid.Health > 0)))) then
					return;
				end;
				for o, F in ipairs(s4) do
					if not _G.FarmPhaBinh then
						break;
					end;
					_tp(F);
					local J = false;
					local D = tick();
					while tick() - D < 12 and (not J and _G.FarmPhaBinh) do
						local o = plr.Character and plr.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart");
						if not o then
							break;
						end;
						local D = (o.Position - F.Position).Magnitude;
						if D <= 3 then
							J = true;
							break;
						end;
						wait(.1);
					end;
					if _G.FarmPhaBinh and J then
						W4("Melee");
						W4("Sword");
						W4("Gun");
					end;
				end;
			end);
		end;
	end;
end);

Toggle = I.Main:AddToggle({
		Name = "Auto Farm Materials",
		Description = "",
		Default = false,
		Callback = function(o)
			(getgenv()).AutoMaterial = o;
		end,
	});
spawn(function()
	local function o(o, F)
		if o:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") and (o:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") and o.Humanoid.Health > 0) then
			if o.Name == F then
				repeat
					wait();
					A.Kill(o, (getgenv()).AutoMaterial);
				until not (getgenv()).AutoMaterial or not o.Parent or o.Humanoid.Health <= 0;
			end;
		end;
	end;
	local function F()
		for o, F in pairs((game:GetService("Workspace"))._WorldOrigin.EnemySpawns:GetChildren()) do
			for o, J in ipairs(MMon) do
				if string.find(F.Name, J) then
					if (game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position - F.Position).Magnitude >= 10 then
						_tp(F.CFrame * Pos);
					end;
				end;
			end;
		end;
	end;
	while wait() do
		if (getgenv()).AutoMaterial then
			pcall(function()
				if (getgenv()).SelectMaterial then
					MaterialMon((getgenv()).SelectMaterial);
					_tp(MPos);
				end;
				for F, J in ipairs(MMon) do
					for F, D in pairs(workspace.Enemies:GetChildren()) do
						o(D, J);
					end;
				end;
				F();
			end);
		end;
	end;
end);

FarmBoss = I.Main:AddToggle({
		Name = "Auto Farm Boss",
		Description = "",
		Default = false,
		Callback = function(o)
			_G.FarmBoss = o;
			spawn(function()
				while wait(Sec) do
					if _G.FarmBoss then
						pcall(function()
							local o = (QuestBeta())[2] ~= nil and (QuestBeta())[3] ~= nil;
							local F = plr.PlayerGui.Main.Quest.Container.QuestTitle.Title.Text;
							if _G.AcceptQuestBoss and o then
								if not string.find(F, (QuestBeta())[0]) then
									replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("AbandonQuest");
								end;
								if plr.PlayerGui.Main.Quest.Visible == false then
									_tp((QuestBeta())[5]);
									if (Root.Position - (QuestBeta())[5].Position).Magnitude <= 5 then
										replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("StartQuest", (QuestBeta())[3], (QuestBeta())[2]);
									end;
								elseif plr.PlayerGui.Main.Quest.Visible == true then
									if workspace.Enemies:FindFirstChild((QuestBeta())[1]) then
										for o, J in pairs(workspace.Enemies:GetChildren()) do
											if A.Alive(J) and J.Name == (QuestBeta())[1] then
												if string.find(F, (QuestBeta())[0]) then
													repeat
														wait();
														A.Kill(J, _G.FarmBoss);
													until not _G.FarmBoss or J.Humanoid.Health <= 0 or not J.Parent or plr.PlayerGui.Main.Quest.Visible == false;
												else
													replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("AbandonQuest");
												end;
											end;
										end;
									else
										_tp((QuestBeta())[4]);
										if replicated:FindFirstChild((QuestBeta())[1]) then
											_tp((replicated:FindFirstChild((QuestBeta())[1])).HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 30, 0));
										end;
									end;
								end;
							else
								if workspace.Enemies:FindFirstChild((QuestBeta())[1]) then
									for o, F in pairs(workspace.Enemies:GetChildren()) do
										if A.Alive(F) and F.Name == (QuestBeta())[1] then
											repeat
												wait();
												A.Kill(F, _G.FarmBoss);
											until not _G.FarmBoss or F.Humanoid.Health <= 0 or not F.Parent;
										end;
									end;
								else
									_tp((QuestBeta())[4]);
									if replicated:FindFirstChild((QuestBeta())[1]) then
										_tp((replicated:FindFirstChild((QuestBeta())[1])).HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 30, 0));
									end;
								end;
							end;
						end);
					end;
				end;
			end);
		end,
	});

FarmAllBoss = I.Main:AddToggle({ Name = "Auto Farm All Boss", Default = false, Callback = function(o)
			_G.AutoFarmAllBoss = o;
		end });
task.spawn(function()
	while task.wait(.3) do
		if _G.AutoFarmAllBoss then
			pcall(function()
				local o = game.Players.LocalPlayer;
				if not o.Character or not o.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
					return;
				end;
				local F = o.Character.HumanoidRootPart;
				local J, D = nil, math.huge;
				for o, G in pairs(workspace.Enemies:GetChildren()) do
					if G:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") and (G:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") and G.Humanoid.Health > 0) then
						if table.find(BossList, G.Name) then
							local o = (F.Position - G.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude;
							if o < D then
								J = G;
								D = o;
							end;
						end;
					end;
				end;
				if J and J:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
					local D = J.HumanoidRootPart;
					local G = J.Humanoid;
					repeat
						task.wait(.1);
						if not _G.AutoFarmAllBoss then
							break;
						end;
						local m = D.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 5, 0);
						if (F.Position - m.Position).Magnitude > 100 then
							o.Character:PivotTo(m);
						else
							_tp(m);
						end;
						if A and typeof(A.Kill) == "function" then
							A.Kill(J, true);
						end;
					until not J.Parent or G.Health <= 0 or not _G.AutoFarmAllBoss;
				end;
			end);
		end;
	end;
end);

									end;

									if GetBP(SwordName) then
										return nil;

I.Settings:AddToggle({ Name = "Auto Hop Server with time", Default = false, Callback = function(o)
		_G.AutoHopServer = o;
		if not o then
			_G.HopTimer = nil;
		end;
	end });
Spawn(function()
	while Wait(1) do
		if _G.AutoHopServer then
			pcall(function()
				if not _G.HopTimer then
					_G.HopTimer = tick();
				end;
				if tick() - _G.HopTimer >= _G.HopDelay then
					_G.HopTimer = tick();
					if syn and syn.queue_on_teleport then
						syn.queue_on_teleport("loadstring(game:HttpGet(\'https://pastefy.app/iiFOhcot/raw\'))()");
					end;
					(game:GetService("TeleportService")):Teleport(game.PlaceId, game.Players.LocalPlayer);
				end;
			end);
		end;
	end;
end);

FishingToggle = I.Fish:AddToggle({
		Name = "Auto Fishing",
		Description = "",
		Default = false,
		Callback = function(o)
			_G.AutoFishing = o;
		end,
	});
local C4 = game:GetService("Players");
local t4 = C4.LocalPlayer;
local Q4 = game:GetService("Workspace");
local h4 = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage");
local d4 = h4:WaitForChild("FishReplicated");
local w4 = d4:WaitForChild("FishingRequest");
local a4 = require(d4.FishingClient.Config);
local z4 = require(h4.Util.GetWaterHeightAtLocation);
local I4 = a4.Rod.MaxLaunchDistance;
task.spawn(function()
	while task.wait(.5) do
		if _G.AutoFishing then
			pcall(function()
				local o = t4.Character or t4.CharacterAdded:Wait();
				local F = o:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart");
				if not F then
					return;
				end;
				local J = o:FindFirstChildOfClass("Tool");
				if _G.SelectedRod and (not J or J.Name ~= _G.SelectedRod) then
					local F = t4.Backpack:FindFirstChild(_G.SelectedRod);
					if F then
						o.Humanoid:EquipTool(F);
						J = F;
					end;
				end;
				if J then
					local D = z4(F.Position);
					local G, m = Q4:FindPartOnRayWithIgnoreList(Ray.new(o.Head.Position, F.CFrame.LookVector * I4), { o, Q4.Characters, Q4.Enemies });
					local X = m and Vector3.new(m.X, math.max(m.Y, D), m.Z);
					local V = J:GetAttribute("State");
					local j = J:GetAttribute("ServerState");
					if X and (V == "ReeledIn" or j == "ReeledIn") then
						w4:InvokeServer("StartCasting");
						task.wait();
						w4:InvokeServer("CastLineAtLocation", X, 100, true);
					elseif j == "Biting" then
						w4:InvokeServer("Catching", true);
						task.wait(.1);
						w4:InvokeServer("Catch", 1);
					end;
				end;
			end);
		end;
	end;
end);

local function O4()
	local o = b4.PlayerGui:FindFirstChild("Quest") or b4.PlayerGui:FindFirstChild("QuestGui");
	if o and (o:FindFirstChild("Container") and o.Container:FindFirstChild("QuestTitle")) then
		return true;
	end;
	return false;
end;

			pcall(function()

					e4:InvokeServer("FishingNPC", "Angler", "AskQuest");
				end;
			end);
		end;
	end;
end);

TravelDress = I.Quests:AddToggle({
		Name = "Auto Quest Sea 2",
		Description = "",
		Default = false,
		Callback = function(o)
			_G.TravelDres = o;
		end,
	});
spawn(function()
	while wait(Sec) do
		pcall(function()
			if _G.TravelDres then
				if plr.Data.Level.Value >= 700 then
					if workspace.Map.Ice.Door.CanCollide == true and workspace.Map.Ice.Door.Transparency == 0 then
						replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("DressrosaQuestProgress", "Detective");
						EquipWeapon("Key");
						repeat
							wait();
							_tp(CFrame.new(1347.7124, 37.3751602, -1325.6488));
						until not _G.TravelDres or Root.Position == (CFrame.new(1347.7124, 37.3751602, -1325.6488)).Position;
					elseif workspace.Map.Ice.Door.CanCollide == false and workspace.Map.Ice.Door.Transparency == 1 then
						if Enemies:FindFirstChild("Ice Admiral") then
							for o, F in pairs(Enemies:GetChildren()) do
								if F.Name == "Ice Admiral" and A.Alive(F) then
									repeat
										task.wait();
										A.Kill(F, _G.TravelDres);
									until _G.TravelDres == false or F.Humanoid.Health <= 0;
									replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("TravelDressrosa");
								end;
							end;
						else
							_tp(CFrame.new(1347.7124, 37.3751602, -1325.6488));
						end;
					else
						replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("TravelDressrosa");
					end;
				end;
			end;
		end);
	end;
end);
Zou = I.Quests:AddToggle({
		Name = "Auto Quest Sea 3",
		Description = "",
		Default = false,
		Callback = function(o)
			_G.AutoZou = o;
		end,
	});
spawn(function()
	while wait(Sec) do
		pcall(function()
			if _G.AutoZou then
				if plr.Data.Level.Value >= 1500 then
					if replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("BartiloQuestProgress", "Bartilo") == 3 then
						if (replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("GetUnlockables")).FlamingoAccess ~= nil then
							replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("F_", "TravelZou");
							if replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("ZQuestProgress", "Check") == 0 then
								local o = GetConnectionEnemies("rip_indra");
								if o then
									repeat
										wait();
										A.Kill(o, _G.AutoZou);
									until not _G.AutoZou or not o.Parent or o.Humanoid.Health <= 0;
									Check = 2;
									repeat
										wait();
										replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("F_", "TravelZou");
									until Check == 1;
								else
									replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("F_", "ZQuestProgress", "Check");
									wait(.1);
									replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("F_", "ZQuestProgress", "Begin");
								end;
							elseif replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("ZQuestProgress", "Check") == 1 then
								replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("F_", "TravelZou");
							else
								local o = GetConnectionEnemies("Don Swan");
								if o then
									repeat
										wait();
										A.Kill(o, _G.AutoZou);
									until not _G.AutoZou or not o.Parent or o.Humanoid.Health <= 0;
								else
									repeat
										wait();
										_tp(CFrame.new(2288.802, 15.1870775, 863.034607));
									until not _G.AutoZou or Root.Position == (CFrame.new(2288.802, 15.1870775, 863.034607)).Position;
									if Root.CFrame == CFrame.new(2288.802, 15.1870775, 863.034607) then
										notween(CFrame.new(2288.802, 15.1870775, 863.034607));
									end;
								end;
							end;
						else
							if (replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("GetUnlockables")).FlamingoAccess == nil then
								TabelDevilFruitStore = {};
								TabelDevilFruitOpen = {};
								for o, F in pairs(replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("getInventoryFruits")) do
									for o, F in pairs(F) do
										if o == "Name" then
											table.insert(TabelDevilFruitStore, F);
										end;
									end;
								end;
								for o, F in next, (game.ReplicatedStorage:WaitForChild("Remotes")).CommF_:InvokeServer("GetFruits") do
									if F.Price >= 1000000 then
										table.insert(TabelDevilFruitOpen, F.Name);
									end;
								end;
								for o, F in pairs(TabelDevilFruitOpen) do
									for o, J in pairs(TabelDevilFruitStore) do
										if F == J and (replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("GetUnlockables")).FlamingoAccess == nil then
											if not plr.Backpack:FindFirstChild(J) then
												replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("F_", "LoadFruit", J);
											else
												replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("F_", "TalkTrevor", "1");
												replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("F_", "TalkTrevor", "2");
												replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("F_", "TalkTrevor", "3");
											end;
										end;
									end;
								end;
								replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("F_", "TalkTrevor", "1");
								replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("F_", "TalkTrevor", "2");
								replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("F_", "TalkTrevor", "3");
							end;
						end;
					else
						if replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("BartiloQuestProgress", "Bartilo") == 0 then
							if string.find(plr.PlayerGui.Main.Quest.Container.QuestTitle.Title.Text, "Swan Pirates") and (string.find(plr.PlayerGui.Main.Quest.Container.QuestTitle.Title.Text, "50") and plr.PlayerGui.Main.Quest.Visible == true) then
								local o = GetConnectionEnemies("Swan Pirate");
								if o then
									pcall(function()
										repeat
											wait();
											A.Kill(o, _G.AutoZou);
										until not o.Parent or o.Humanoid.Health <= 0 or _G.AutoZou == false or plr.PlayerGui.Main.Quest.Visible == false;
									end);
								else
									_tp(CFrame.new(1057.92761, 137.614319, 1242.08069));
								end;
							else
								_tp(CFrame.new(-456.28952, 73.0200958, 299.895966));
							end;
						elseif replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("BartiloQuestProgress", "Bartilo") == 1 then
							local o = GetConnectionEnemies("Jeremy");
							if o then
								repeat
									wait();
									A.Kill(o, _G.AutoZou);
								until not o.Parent or o.Humanoid.Health <= 0 or _G.AutoZou == false;
							else
								_tp(CFrame.new(2099.88159, 448.931, 648.997375));
							end;
						elseif replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("BartiloQuestProgress", "Bartilo") == 2 then
							repeat
								wait();
								_tp(CFrame.new(-1836, 11, 1714));
							until not _G.AutoZou or Root.Position == (CFrame.new(-1836, 11, 1714)).Position;
							if Root.CFrame == CFrame.new(-1836, 11, 1714) then
								notween(CFrame.new(-1836, 11, 1714));
							end;
							notween(CFrame.new(-1850.49329, 13.1789551, 1750.89685));
							wait(.1);
							notween(CFrame.new(-1858.87305, 19.3777466, 1712.01807));
							wait(.1);
							notween(CFrame.new(-1803.94324, 16.5789185, 1750.89685));
							wait(.1);
							notween(CFrame.new(-1858.55835, 16.8604317, 1724.79541));
							wait(.1);
							notween(CFrame.new(-1869.54224, 15.987854, 1681.00659));
							wait(.1);
							notween(CFrame.new(-1800.0979, 16.4978027, 1684.52368));
							wait(.1);
							notween(CFrame.new(-1819.26343, 14.795166, 1717.90625));
							wait(.1);
							notween(CFrame.new(-1813.51843, 14.8604736, 1724.79541));
						end;
					end;
				end;
			end;
		end);
	end;
end);

	while wait(.2) do

			if Quest1 == true then
				T4:SetDesc("Quest Number : Quest1");
			elseif Quest2 == true then
				T4:SetDesc("Quest Number : Quest2");

				T4:SetDesc("Quest Number : Quest3");

				T4:SetDesc("Quest Number : Quest4");

task.spawn(function()
	while wait() do
		if _G.Auto_Soul_Guitar then
			pcall(function()
				local o = GetConnectionEnemies("Living Zombie");
				if o then
					o.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(-10138.397460938, 138.65246582031, 5902.8920898438);
					o.Head.CanCollide = false;
					o.Humanoid.Sit = false;
					o.HumanoidRootPart.CanCollide = false;
					o.Humanoid.JumpPower = 0;
					o.Humanoid.WalkSpeed = 0;
					if o.Humanoid:FindFirstChild("Animator") then
						(o.Humanoid:FindFirstChild("Animator")):Destroy();
					end;
				end;
			end);
		end;
	end;
end);
function getT(o)
	local F;
	if o == 1 then
		F = workspace.Map["Haunted Castle"].Tablet.Segment1.Line.Rotation;
	elseif o == 3 then
		F = workspace.Map["Haunted Castle"].Tablet.Segment3.Line.Rotation;
	elseif o == 4 then
		F = workspace.Map["Haunted Castle"].Tablet.Segment4.Line.Rotation;
	elseif o == 7 then
		F = workspace.Map["Haunted Castle"].Tablet.Segment7.Line.Rotation;
	elseif o == 10 then
		F = workspace.Map["Haunted Castle"].Tablet.Segment10.Line.Rotation;
	end;
	if F then
		return F.Z;
	end;
end;
function getRT(o)
	local F = workspace.Map["Haunted Castle"].Trophies.Quest;
	local J;
	for F, D in pairs(F:GetChildren()) do
		if o == 1 and (D.Name == "Trophy1" and D:FindFirstChild("Handle")) then
			J = D.Handle.Rotation;
		elseif o == 2 and (D.Name == "Trophy2" and D:FindFirstChild("Handle")) then
			J = D.Handle.Rotation;
		elseif o == 3 and (D.Name == "Trophy3" and D:FindFirstChild("Handle")) then
			J = D.Handle.Rotation;
		elseif o == 4 and (D.Name == "Trophy4" and D:FindFirstChild("Handle")) then
			J = D.Handle.Rotation;
		elseif o == 5 and (D.Name == "Trophy5" and D:FindFirstChild("Handle")) then
			J = D.Handle.Rotation;
		end;
		if J then
			return J.Z;
		end;
	end;
end;
GetFirePlacard = function(o, F)
		if tostring(workspace.Map["Haunted Castle"]["Placard" .. o][F].Indicator.BrickColor) ~= "Pearl" then
			fireclickdetector(workspace.Map["Haunted Castle"]["Placard" .. o][F].ClickDetector);
		end;
	end;

	Name = "Auto Farm Material Skull Guitar",
	Description = "",
	Default = false,
	Callback = function(o)
		_G.AutoMatSoul = o;
	end,
});
spawn(function()
	while wait(Sec) do
		pcall(function()
			if _G.AutoMatSoul and GetWP("Skull Guitar") == false then
				if GetM("Bones") >= 500 and (GetM("Ectoplasm") >= 250 and GetM("Dark Fragment") >= 1) then
					replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("soulGuitarBuy", true);
				else
					if GetM("Ectoplasm") <= 250 then
						if _G.AutoMatSoul and World2 then
							local o = {
									"Ship Deckhand",
									"Ship Engineer",
									"Ship Steward",
									"Ship Officer",
									"Arctic Warrior",
								};
							local F = GetConnectionEnemies(o);
							if F then
								repeat
									task.wait();
									A.Kill(F, _G.AutoMatSoul);
								until not _G.AutoMatSoul or not F.Parent or F.Humanoid.Health <= 0;
							else
								replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("requestEntrance", Vector3.new(923.21252441406, 126.9760055542, 32852.83203125));
							end;
						else
							replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("TravelDressrosa");
						end;
					elseif GetM("Dark Fragment") < 1 then
						if _G.AutoMatSoul and World2 then
							local o = GetConnectionEnemies("Darkbeard");
							if o then
								repeat
									task.wait();
									A.Kill(o, _G.AutoMatSoul);
								until _G.AutoMatSoul or o.Humanoid.Health <= 0;
							else
								_tp(CFrame.new(3798.4575195313, 13.826690673828, -3399.806640625));
							end;
						else
							replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("TravelDressrosa");
						end;
						if not GetConnectionEnemies("Darkbeard") then
							Hop();
						end;
					elseif GetM("Bones") <= 500 then
						if _G.AutoMatSoul and World3 then
							local o = {
									"Reborn Skeleton",
									"Living Zombie",
									"Demonic Soul",
									"Posessed Mummy",
								};
							local F = GetConnectionEnemies(o);
							if F then
								repeat
									task.wait();
									A.Kill(F, _G.AutoMatSoul);
								until not _G.AutoMatSoul or F.Humanoid.Health <= 0 or not F.Parent or F.Humanoid.Health <= 0;
							else
								_tp(CFrame.new(-9504.8564453125, 172.14292907715, 6057.259765625));
							end;
						else
							replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("TravelZou");
						end;
					end;
				end;
			end;
		end);
	end;
end);

Q = I.Quests:AddToggle({
		Name = "Auto Tushita CDK",
		Description = "",
		Default = false,
		Callback = function(o)
			_G.CDK_TS = o;
		end,
	});
spawn(function()
	while wait() do
		pcall(function()
			if _G.CDK_TS then
				if tostring(replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("CDKQuest", "OpenDoor")) ~= "opened" then
					wait(.7);
					replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("CDKQuest", "OpenDoor");
					wait(.3);
					replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("CDKQuest", "OpenDoor", true);
				else
					if (replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("CDKQuest", "Progress")).Finished == nil then
						replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("CDKQuest", "StartTrial", "Good");
					elseif (replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("CDKQuest", "Progress")).Finished == false then
						if tonumber((replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("CDKQuest", "Progress")).Good) == -3 then
							QuestTushita_1 = true;
							QuestTushita_2 = false;
							QuestTushita_3 = false;
							repeat
								wait();
								_tp(CFrame.new(-4602.5107421875, 16.446542739868, -2880.998046875));
							until ((CFrame.new(-4602.5107421875, 16.446542739868, -2880.998046875)).Position - (game:GetService("Players")).LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude <= 3 or not _G.CDK_TS or tonumber((replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("CDKQuest", "Progress")).Good) == 1;
							if ((CFrame.new(-4602.5107421875, 16.446542739868, -2880.998046875)).Position - (game:GetService("Players")).LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude <= 10 then
								wait(.7);
								replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("CDKQuest", "BoatQuest", workspace.NPCs:FindFirstChild("Luxury Boat Dealer"), "Check");
								wait(.5);
								replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("CDKQuest", "BoatQuest", workspace.NPCs:FindFirstChild("Luxury Boat Dealer"));
							end;
							wait(1);
							repeat
								wait();
								_tp(CFrame.new(4001.1853027344, 10.089399337769, -2654.86328125));
							until ((CFrame.new(4001.1853027344, 10.089399337769, -2654.86328125)).Position - (game:GetService("Players")).LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude <= 3 or not _G.CDK_TS or tonumber((replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("CDKQuest", "Progress")).Good) == 1;
							if ((CFrame.new(4001.1853027344, 10.089399337769, -2654.86328125)).Position - (game:GetService("Players")).LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude <= 10 then
								wait(.7);
								replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("CDKQuest", "BoatQuest", workspace.NPCs:FindFirstChild("Luxury Boat Dealer"), "Check");
								wait(.5);
								replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("CDKQuest", "BoatQuest", workspace.NPCs:FindFirstChild("Luxury Boat Dealer"));
							end;
							wait(1);
							repeat
								wait();
								_tp(CFrame.new(-9530.763671875, 7.2452087402344, -8375.5087890625));
							until ((CFrame.new(-9530.763671875, 7.2452087402344, -8375.5087890625)).Position - (game:GetService("Players")).LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude <= 3 or not _G.CDK_TS or tonumber((replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("CDKQuest", "Progress")).Good) == 1;
							if ((CFrame.new(-9530.763671875, 7.2452087402344, -8375.5087890625)).Position - (game:GetService("Players")).LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude <= 10 then
								wait(.7);
								replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("CDKQuest", "BoatQuest", workspace.NPCs:FindFirstChild("Luxury Boat Dealer"), "Check");
								wait(.5);
								replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("CDKQuest", "BoatQuest", workspace.NPCs:FindFirstChild("Luxury Boat Dealer"));
							end;
							wait(1);
						elseif tonumber((replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("CDKQuest", "Progress")).Good) == -4 then
							QuestTushita_1 = false;
							QuestTushita_2 = true;
							QuestTushita_3 = false;
							repeat
								wait();
								_G.AutoRaidCastle = true;
							until not _G.CDK_TS or tonumber((replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("CDKQuest", "Progress")).Good) == 2;
							_G.AutoRaidCastle = false;
						elseif tonumber((replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("CDKQuest", "Progress")).Good) == -5 then
							QuestTushita_1 = false;
							QuestTushita_2 = false;
							QuestTushita_3 = true;
							if workspace.Enemies:FindFirstChild("Cake Queen") then
								for o, F in pairs(workspace.Enemies:GetChildren()) do
									if F.Name == "Cake Queen" then
										if F:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") and (F:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") and F.Humanoid.Health > 0) then
											repeat
												wait();
												A.Kill(F, _G.CDK_TS);
											until not _G.CDK_TS or not F.Parent or F.Humanoid.Health <= 0 or tonumber((replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("CDKQuest", "Progress")).Good) == 3;
										end;
									end;
								end;
							elseif replicated:FindFirstChild("Cake Queen") and (replicated:FindFirstChild("Cake Queen")).Humanoid.Health > 0 then
								_tp((replicated:FindFirstChild("Cake Queen")).HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 30, 0));
							else
								if (game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position - workspace.Map.HeavenlyDimension.Spawn.Position).Magnitude <= 1000 then
									for o, F in pairs(workspace.Map.HeavenlyDimension.Exit:GetChildren()) do
										Ex = o;
									end;
									if Ex == 2 then
										repeat
											wait();
											game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = workspace.Map.HeavenlyDimension.Exit.CFrame;
										until not _G.CDK_TS or tonumber((replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("CDKQuest", "Progress")).Good) == 3;
									end;
									repeat
										wait();
										repeat
											wait();
											_tp(CFrame.new(-22529.6171875, 5275.7739257812, 3873.5712890625));
											for o, F in pairs(workspace.Map.HeavenlyDimension:GetDescendants()) do
												if F:IsA("ProximityPrompt") then
													fireproximityprompt(F);
												end;
											end;
										until ((CFrame.new(-22529.6171875, 5275.7739257812, 3873.5712890625)).Position - game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude < 5;
										wait(2);
										_G.DoneT1 = true;
									until not _G.CDK_TS or _G.DoneT1;
									repeat
										wait();
										repeat
											wait();
											_tp(CFrame.new(-22637.291015625, 5281.365234375, 3749.2885742188));
											for o, F in pairs(workspace.Map.HeavenlyDimension:GetDescendants()) do
												if F:IsA("ProximityPrompt") then
													fireproximityprompt(F);
												end;
											end;
										until ((CFrame.new(-22637.291015625, 5281.365234375, 3749.2885742188)).Position - game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude < 5;
										wait(2);
										_G.DoneT2 = true;
									until _G.DoneT2 or _G.CDK_TS == false;
									repeat
										wait();
										repeat
											task.wait();
											_tp(CFrame.new(-22791.14453125, 5277.1655273438, 3764.5700683594));
											for o, F in pairs(workspace.Map.HeavenlyDimension:GetDescendants()) do
												if F:IsA("ProximityPrompt") then
													fireproximityprompt(F);
												end;
											end;
										until ((CFrame.new(-22791.14453125, 5277.1655273438, 3764.5700683594)).Position - game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude < 5;
										wait(2);
										_G.DoneT3 = true;
									until _G.DoneT3 or _G.CDK_TS == false;
									for o, F in pairs(workspace.Enemies:GetChildren()) do
										if ((F:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart")).Position - (CFrame.new(-22695.7012, 5270.93652, 3814.42847, .11794927, 3.32185834e-008, .99301964, -8.73070718e-008, 1, -2.30819008e-008, -0.99301964, -8.3975138e-008, .11794927)).Position).Magnitude <= 300 then
											if F:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") and (F:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") and (F:FindFirstChild("Humanoid")).Health > 0) then
												repeat
													wait();
													A.Kill(F, _G.CDK_TS);
												until not _G.CDK_TS or F.Humanoid.Health <= 0 or not F.Parent;
											end;
										end;
									end;
								end;
							end;
						end;
					end;
				end;
			end;
		end);
	end;
end);

				for o, F in pairs(replicated.NPCs:GetChildren()) do
