Q = I.Quests:AddToggle({
		Name = "Auto Pole V1",
		Description = "",
		Default = false,
		Callback = function(o)
			_G.AutoPole = o;
		end,
	});
spawn(function()
	while wait(Sec) do
		if _G.AutoPole then
			pcall(function()
				local o = GetConnectionEnemies("Thunder God");
				if o then
					repeat
						task.wait();
						A.Kill(o, _G.AutoPole);
					until not _G.AutoPole or not o.Parent or o.Humanoid.Health <= 0;
				else
					_tp(CFrame.new(-7994.984375, 5761.025390625, -2088.6479492188));
				end;
			end);
		end;
	end;
end);
Q = I.Quests:AddToggle({
		Name = "Auto Pole V2 [Beta]",
		Description = "",
		Default = false,
		Callback = function(o)
			_G.AutoPoleV2 = o;
		end,
	});
spawn(function()
	while wait(Sec) do
		pcall(function()
			if _G.AutoPoleV2 then
				if not GetBP("Pole (1st Form)") then
					replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("LoadItem", "Pole (1st Form)");
				end;
				if not GetBP("Pole (2nd Form)") then
					replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("LoadItem", "Pole (2nd Form)");
				end;
				if GetBP("Pole (1st Form)") and (GetBP("Pole (1st Form)")).Level.Value <= 179 then
					_G.Level = true;
				elseif GetBP("Pole (1st Form)") and (GetBP("Pole (1st Form)")).Level.Value >= 180 then
					_G.Level = false;
				end;
				if not GetBP("Rumble Fruit") then
					return;
				end;
				if (GetBP("Rumble Fruit")).AwakenedMoves:FindFirstChild("Z") and ((GetBP("Rumble Fruit")).AwakenedMoves:FindFirstChild("X") and ((GetBP("Rumble Fruit")).AwakenedMoves:FindFirstChild("C") and ((GetBP("Rumble Fruit")).AwakenedMoves:FindFirstChild("V") and (GetBP("Rumble Fruit")).AwakenedMoves:FindFirstChild("F")))) then
					_G.SelectChip = nil;
					_G.Raiding = false;
					_G.Auto_Awakener = false;
					if plr.Data.Fragments.Value >= 5000 then
						replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("Thunder God", "Talk");
						wait(Sec);
						replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("Thunder God", "Sure");
					end;
				elseif replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("Awakener", "Check") == nil or replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("Awakener", "Check") == 0 then
					_G.SelectChip = "Rumble";
					local o = replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("RaidsNpc", "Select", _G.SelectChip);
					if o then
						o:Stop();
					end;
					_G.Raiding = true;
					_G.Auto_Awakener = true;
				end;
			end;
		end);
	end;
end);

Q = I.Quests:AddToggle({
		Name = "Auto Saber Sword",
		Description = "",
		Default = false,
		Callback = function(o)
			_G.AutoSaber = o;
		end,
	});
spawn(function()
	while wait(.2) do
		pcall(function()
			if _G.AutoSaber and (plr.Data.Level.Value >= 200 and (not plr.Backpack:FindFirstChild("Saber") and not plr.Character:FindFirstChild("Saber"))) then
				if workspace.Map.Jungle.Final.Part.Transparency == 0 then
					if workspace.Map.Jungle.QuestPlates.Door.Transparency == 0 then
						if ((CFrame.new(-1612.55884, 36.9774132, 148.719543, .37091279, 3.0717151e-009, -0.928667724, 3.97099491e-008, 1, 1.91679348e-008, .928667724, -4.39869794e-008, .37091279)).Position - plr.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude <= 100 then
							_tp(plr.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame);
							wait(.5);
							plr.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = workspace.Map.Jungle.QuestPlates.Plate1.Button.CFrame;
							wait(.5);
							plr.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = workspace.Map.Jungle.QuestPlates.Plate2.Button.CFrame;
							wait(.5);
							plr.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = workspace.Map.Jungle.QuestPlates.Plate3.Button.CFrame;
							wait(.5);
							plr.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = workspace.Map.Jungle.QuestPlates.Plate4.Button.CFrame;
							wait(.5);
							plr.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = workspace.Map.Jungle.QuestPlates.Plate5.Button.CFrame;
							wait(.5);
						else
							_tp(CFrame.new(-1612.55884, 36.9774132, 148.719543, .37091279, 3.0717151e-009, -0.928667724, 3.97099491e-008, 1, 1.91679348e-008, .928667724, -4.39869794e-008, .37091279));
						end;
					else
						if workspace.Map.Desert.Burn.Part.Transparency == 0 then
							if plr.Backpack:FindFirstChild("Torch") or plr.Character:FindFirstChild("Torch") then
								EquipWeapon("Torch");
								firetouchinterest(plr.Character.Torch.Handle, workspace.Map.Desert.Burn.Fire, 0);
								firetouchinterest(plr.Character.Torch.Handle, workspace.Map.Desert.Burn.Fire, 1);
								_tp(CFrame.new(1114.61475, 5.04679728, 4350.22803, -0.648466587, -1.28799094e-009, .761243105, -5.70652914e-010, 1, 1.20584542e-009, -0.761243105, 3.47544882e-010, -0.648466587));
							else
								_tp(CFrame.new(-1610.00757, 11.5049858, 164.001587, .984807551, -0.167722285, -0.0449818149, .17364943, .951244235, .254912198, 3.42372805e-005, -0.258850515, .965917408));
							end;
						else
							if replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("ProQuestProgress", "SickMan") ~= 0 then
								replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("ProQuestProgress", "GetCup");
								wait(.5);
								EquipWeapon("Cup");
								wait(.5);
								replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("ProQuestProgress", "FillCup", plr.Character.Cup);
								wait(Sec);
								replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("ProQuestProgress", "SickMan");
							else
								if replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("ProQuestProgress", "RichSon") == nil then
									replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("ProQuestProgress", "RichSon");
								elseif replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("ProQuestProgress", "RichSon") == 0 then
									if workspace.Enemies:FindFirstChild("Mob Leader") or replicated:FindFirstChild("Mob Leader") then
										_tp(CFrame.new(-2967.59521, -4.91089821, 5328.70703, .342208564, -0.0227849055, .939347804, .0251603816, .999569714, .0150796166, -0.939287126, .0184739735, .342634559));
										for o, F in pairs(workspace.Enemies:GetChildren()) do
											if F.Name == "Mob Leader" and A.Alive(F) then
												repeat
													task.wait();
													A.Kill(F, _G.AutoSaber);
												until F.Humanoid.Health <= 0 or _G.AutoSaber == false;
											end;
										end;
									end;
								elseif replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("ProQuestProgress", "RichSon") == 1 then
									replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("ProQuestProgress", "RichSon");
									EquipWeapon("Relic");
									_tp(CFrame.new(-1404.91504, 29.9773273, 3.80598116, .876514494, 5.66906877e-009, .481375456, 2.53851997e-008, 1, -5.79995607e-008, -0.481375456, 6.30572643e-008, .876514494));
								end;
							end;
						end;
					end;
				else
					if workspace.Enemies:FindFirstChild("Saber Expert") or replicated:FindFirstChild("Saber Expert") then
						for o, F in pairs(workspace.Enemies:GetChildren()) do
							if F.Name == "Saber Expert" and A.Alive(F) then
								repeat
									task.wait();
									A.Kill(F, _G.AutoSaber);
								until F.Humanoid.Health <= 0 or _G.AutoSaber == false;
								if F.Humanoid.Health <= 0 then
									replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("ProQuestProgress", "PlaceRelic");
								end;
							end;
						end;
					else
						_tp(CFrame.new(-1401.85046, 29.9773273, 8.81916237, .85820812, 8.76083845e-008, .513301849, -8.55007443e-008, 1, -2.77243419e-008, -0.513301849, -2.00944328e-008, .85820812));
					end;
				end;
			end;
		end);
	end;
end);

Q = I.Quests:AddToggle({
		Name = "Auto Usoap\'s Hat",
		Description = "",
		Default = false,
		Callback = function(o)
			_G.AutoGetUsoap = o;
		end,
	});
spawn(function()
	while task.wait(Sec) do
		pcall(function()
			if _G.AutoGetUsoap then
				for o, F in pairs(workspace.Characters:GetChildren()) do
					if F.Name ~= plr.Name then
						if F.Humanoid.Health > 0 and (F:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") and (F.Parent and (Root.Position - F.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude <= 230)) then
							repeat
								task.wait();
								EquipWeapon(_G.SelectWeapon);
								_tp(F.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(1, 1, 2));
							until _G.AutoGetUsoap == false or F.Humanoid.Health <= 0 or not F.Parent or not F:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") or not F:FindFirstChild("Humanoid");
						end;
					end;
				end;
			end;
		end);
	end;
end);

Q = I.Quests:AddToggle({
		Name = "Auto Unlocked DonSwan",
		Description = "",
		Default = false,
		Callback = function(o)
			_G.Auto_DonAcces = o;
		end,
	});
spawn(function()
	while wait(.1) do
		if _G.Auto_DonAcces then
			pcall(function()
				if (replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("GetUnlockables")).FlamingoAccess == nil and plr.Data.Level.Value >= 1500 then
					FruitPrice = {};
					FruitStore = {};
					for o, F in next, (replicated:WaitForChild("Remotes")).CommF_:InvokeServer("GetFruits") do
						if F.Price >= 1000000 then
							table.insert(FruitPrice, F.Name);
						end;
					end;
					for o, F in pairs(replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("getInventoryFruits")) do
						for o, F in pairs(F) do
							if o == "Name" then
								table.insert(FruitStore, F);
							end;
						end;
						replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("Cousin", "Buy");
						for o, F in pairs(FruitPrice) do
							for o, J in pairs(FruitStore) do
								if F == J and (replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("GetUnlockables")).FlamingoAccess == nil then
									_G.StoreF = false;
									if not plr.Backpack:FindFirstChild(FruitStore) then
										replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("LoadFruit", tostring(F));
									else
										replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("TalkTrevor", "1");
										replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("TalkTrevor", "2");
										replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("TalkTrevor", "3");
									end;
								end;
							end;
						end;
						if (replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("GetUnlockables")).FlamingoAccess ~= nil then
							_G.StoreF = true;
							_G.Auto_DonAcces = false;
						end;
					end;
				end;
			end);
		end;
	end;
end);

		pcall(function()
			if _G.obsFarm then
				replicated.Remotes.CommE:FireServer("Ken", true);
				if plr:GetAttribute("KenDodgesLeft") == 0 then
					KenTest = false;
				elseif plr:GetAttribute("KenDodgesLeft") > 0 then
					replicated.Remotes.CommE:FireServer("Ken", true);
					KenTest = true;
				end;
			end;
		end);
	end;

spawn(function()
	while wait(.2) do
		pcall(function()
			if _G.obsFarm then
				if World1 then
					if workspace.Enemies:FindFirstChild("Galley Captain") then
						if KenTest then
							repeat
								wait();
								plr.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = (workspace.Enemies:FindFirstChild("Galley Captain")).HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(3, 0, 0);
							until _G.obsFarm == false or KenTest == false;
						else
							repeat
								wait();
								plr.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = (workspace.Enemies:FindFirstChild("Galley Captain")).HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 50, 0);
							until _G.obsFarm == false or KenTest;
						end;
					else
						_tp(CFrame.new(5533.29785, 88.1079102, 4852.3916));
					end;
				elseif World2 then
					if workspace.Enemies:FindFirstChild("Lava Pirate") then
						if KenTest then
							repeat
								wait();

						replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("Bones", "Buy", 1, 1);
						replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("BuyDragonTalon");
					elseif GetBP("Dragon Claw") and (GetBP("Dragon Claw")).Level.Value < 400 then
						repeat
							_G.AutoFarm_Bone = true;
							wait();
						until not _G.AutoDragonTalon or GetBP("Dragon Talon");
						_G.AutoFarm_Bone = false;
					end;
				end;
			end);
		end;
	end;
end);

		Description = "",

			_G.Snaguine = o;
		end,

spawn(function()
	while wait(Sec) do
		if _G.Snaguine then
			pcall(function()
				if not GetBP("Sanguine Art") then
					replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("Sanguine Art");
				end;
				if not GetBP("Sanguine Art") then
					if GetM("Leviathan Heart") >= 1 then
						print("Completed!!");
					else
						if World3 then
							_G.DangerSc = "Lv Infinite";
							_G.SailBoats = true;
						else
							_G.SailBoats = false;
						end;
					end;
					if GetM("Vampire Fang") <= 19 then
						if World2 then
							local o = GetConnectionEnemies("Vampire");
							if o then
								repeat
									task.wait();
									A.Kill(o, _G.Snaguine);
								until not _G.Snaguine or o.Humanoid.Health <= 0 or not o.Parent;
							else
								_tp(CFrame.new(-6041.2924804688, 6.4027109146118, -1304.6333007812));
							end;
						else
							replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("TravelDressrosa");
						end;
					end;
					if GetM("Vampire Fang") >= 20 and GetM("Demonic Wisp") <= 19 then
						if World3 then
							local o = GetConnectionEnemies("Demonic Soul");
							if o then
								repeat
									task.wait();
									A.Kill(o, _G.Snaguine);
								until not _G.Snaguine or o.Humanoid.Health <= 0 or not o.Parent;
							else
								_tp(CFrame.new(-9495.6806640625, 453.58624267578, 5977.3486328125));
							end;
						else
							replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("TravelZou");
						end;
					end;
					if GetM("Vampire Fang") >= 20 and (GetM("Demonic Wisp") >= 20 and GetM("Dark Fragment") <= 1) then
						if World2 then
							local o = GetConnectionEnemies("Darkbeard");
							if o then
								repeat
									task.wait();
									A.Kill(black, _G.Snaguine);
								until _G.Snaguine or black.Humanoid.Health <= 0 or not black.Parent;
							else
								_tp(CFrame.new(3798.4575195313, 13.826690673828, -3399.806640625));
							end;
						else
							replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("TravelDressrosa");
						end;
					end;
				else
					replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("BuySanguineArt");
				end;
			end);
		end;
	end;
end);

spawn(function()
	while wait(.2) do
		pcall(function()
			local o = "http://www.roblox.com/asset/?id=9709150401";
			local F = "http://www.roblox.com/asset/?id=9709150086";
			local J = "http://www.roblox.com/asset/?id=9709149680";
			local D = "http://www.roblox.com/asset/?id=9709149431";
			local G = "http://www.roblox.com/asset/?id=9709149052";
			local m = "http://www.roblox.com/asset/?id=9709143733";
			local X = "http://www.roblox.com/asset/?id=9709139597";
			local V = "http://www.roblox.com/asset/?id=9709135895";
			local j = Getmoon();
			if j == V then
				f4:SetDesc("Moon : 0 / 8");
			elseif j == X then
				f4:SetDesc("Moon : 1 / 8");
			elseif j == m then
				f4:SetDesc("Moon : 2 / 8");
			elseif j == G then
				f4:SetDesc("Moon : 3 / 8 [ Next Night ]");
			elseif j == D then
				f4:SetDesc("Moon : 4 / 8 [ Full Moon ]");
			elseif j == J then
				f4:SetDesc("Moon : 5 / 8 [ Last Night ]");
			elseif j == F then
				f4:SetDesc("Moon : 6 / 8");
			elseif j == o then
				f4:SetDesc("Moon : 7 / 8");
			end;
		end);
	end;
end);
I.Race:AddToggle({
	Name = "Auto Find Mirage Island",
	Description = "",
	Default = false,
	Callback = function(o)
		_G.FindMirage = o;
	end,
});
spawn(function()
	while wait() do
		if _G.FindMirage then
			pcall(function()
				if not workspace._WorldOrigin.Locations:FindFirstChild("Mirage Island", true) then
					local o = CheckBoat();
					if not o then
						local o = CFrame.new(-16927.451, 9.086, 433.864);
						TeleportToTarget(o);
						if (o.Position - plr.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude <= 10 then
							replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("BuyBoat", _G.SelectedBoat);
						end;
					else
						if plr.Character.Humanoid.Sit == false then
							local F = o.VehicleSeat.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 1, 0);
							_tp(F);
						else
							repeat
								wait();
								local o = CFrame.new(-10000000, 31, 37016.25);
								if CheckEnemiesBoat() or CheckTerrorShark() or CheckPirateGrandBrigade() then
									_tp(CFrame.new(-10000000, 150, 37016.25));
								else
									_tp(CFrame.new(-10000000, 31, 37016.25));
								end;
							until not _G.FindMirage or (o.Position - plr.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude <= 10 or workspace._WorldOrigin.Locations:FindFirstChild("Mirage Island") or plr.Character.Humanoid.Sit == false;
							plr.Character.Humanoid.Sit = false;
						end;
					end;
				else
					_tp(workspace.Map.MysticIsland.Center.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 300, 0));
				end;
			end);
		end;
	end;
end);

I.Race:AddToggle({
	Name = "Auto Collect Mirage Chest",
	Description = "",
	Default = false,
	Callback = function(o)
		_G.FarmChestM = o;
	end,
});
spawn(function()
	while wait(.2) do
		if _G.FarmChestM then
			pcall(function()
				if workspace.Map.MysticIsland.Chests:FindFirstChild("DiamondChest") or workspace.Map.MysticIsland.Chests:FindFirstChild("FragChest") then
					local o = game:GetService("CollectionService");
					local F = game:GetService("Players");
					local J = F.LocalPlayer;
					local D = J.Character or J.CharacterAdded:Wait();
					if not D then
						return;
					end;
					local G = (D:GetPivot()).Position;
					local m = o:GetTagged("_ChestTagged");
					local X, V = math.huge, nil;
					for o = 1, #m, 1 do
						local F = m[o];
						local J = ((F:GetPivot()).Position - G).Magnitude;
						if not SelectedIsland or F:IsDescendantOf(SelectedIsland) then
							if not F:GetAttribute("IsDisabled") and J < X then
								X = J;
								V = F;
							end;
						end;
					end;
					if V then
						_tp(V:GetPivot());
					end;
				end;
			end);
		end;
	end;
end);

function MoveCamtoMoon()
	workspace.CurrentCamera.CFrame = CFrame.new(workspace.CurrentCamera.CFrame.Position, Lighting:GetMoonDirection() + workspace.CurrentCamera.CFrame.Position);
	plr.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(plr.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position, Lighting:GetMoonDirection() + plr.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame.Position);
end;
task.spawn(function()
	while task.wait() do
		if LookM then
			MoveCamtoMoon();
			wait(.1);
			replicated.Remotes.CommE:FireServer("ActivateAbility");
		end;
	end;
end);

	Description = "",

	Callback = function(o)
		LookMV3 = o;
	end,

function MoveCamtoMoon()
	local o = Lighting:GetMoonDirection();
	workspace.CurrentCamera.CFrame = CFrame.new(workspace.CurrentCamera.CFrame.Position, workspace.CurrentCamera.CFrame.Position + o);
	plr.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = CFrame.new(plr.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position, plr.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position + o);
end;

	while task.wait(.1) do
		if LookMV3 then
			MoveCamtoMoon();
			replicated.Remotes.CommE:FireServer("ActivateAbility");
			UIS:SendKeyEvent(true, "T", false, game);
			wait(.5);
			UIS:SendKeyEvent(false, "T", false, game);
		end;
	end;
end);

						replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("Alchemist", "2");
					elseif replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("Alchemist", "1") == 1 then
						if not plr.Backpack:FindFirstChild("Flower 1") and not plr.Character:FindFirstChild("Flower 1") then
							_tp(workspace.Flower1.CFrame);
						elseif not plr.Backpack:FindFirstChild("Flower 2") and not plr.Character:FindFirstChild("Flower 2") then
							_tp(workspace.Flower2.CFrame);
						elseif not plr.Backpack:FindFirstChild("Flower 3") and not plr.Character:FindFirstChild("Flower 3") then
							local o = GetConnectionEnemies("Swan Pirate");
							if o then
								repeat
									wait();
									A.Kill(o, _G.Auto_Fish);
								until plr.Backpack:FindFirstChild("Flower 3") or not o.Parent or o.Humanoid.Health <= 0 or _G.Auto_Fish == false;
							else
								_tp(CFrame.new(980.09851074219, 121.33129882812, 1287.2093505859));
							end;
						end;
					elseif replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("Alchemist", "1") == 2 then
						replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("Alchemist", "3");
					end;
				elseif replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("Wenlocktoad", "1") == 0 then
					replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("Wenlocktoad", "2");
				elseif replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("Wenlocktoad", "1") == 1 then
					warn("Sea Beast Soon");
				end;
			end;
		end);
	end;
end);

Trials = I.Race:AddToggle({
		Name = "Auto Complete Trial Race",
		Description = "",
		Default = false,
		Callback = function(o)
			_G.Complete_Trials = o;
		end,

GetSeaBeastTrial = function()
		if not workspace.Map:FindFirstChild("FishmanTrial") then
			return nil;
		end;
		if workspace._WorldOrigin.Locations:FindFirstChild("Trial of Water") then
			FishmanTrial = workspace._WorldOrigin.Locations:FindFirstChild("Trial of Water");
		end;
		if FishmanTrial then
			for o, F in next, workspace.SeaBeasts:GetChildren() do
				if F:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") and (F.HumanoidRootPart.Position - FishmanTrial.Position).Magnitude <= 1500 then
					if F.Health.Value > 0 then
						return F;
					end;
				end;
			end;
		end;
	end;
spawn(function()
	while wait(Sec) do
		pcall(function()
			if _G.Complete_Trials then
				if tostring(plr.Data.Race.Value) == "Mink" then
					notween(workspace.Map.MinkTrial.Ceiling.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, -20, 0));
				end;
			end;
		end);
	end;
end);
spawn(function()
	while wait(Sec) do
		pcall(function()
			if _G.Complete_Trials then
				if tostring(plr.Data.Race.Value) == "Fishman" then
					if GetSeaBeastTrial() then
						repeat
							task.wait();
							spawn(function()
								_tp(CFrame.new((GetSeaBeastTrial()).HumanoidRootPart.Position.X, (game:GetService("Workspace")).Map["WaterBase-Plane"].Position.Y + 300, (GetSeaBeastTrial()).HumanoidRootPart.Position.Z));
							end);
							MousePos = (GetSeaBeastTrial()).HumanoidRootPart.Position;
							Useskills("Melee", "Z");
							Useskills("Melee", "X");
							Useskills("Melee", "C");
							wait(.1);
							Useskills("Sword", "Z");
							Useskills("Sword", "X");
							wait(.1);
							Useskills("Blox Fruit", "Z");
							Useskills("Blox Fruit", "X");
							Useskills("Blox Fruit", "C");
							wait(.1);
							Useskills("Gun", "Z");
							Useskills("Gun", "X");
						until _G.Complete_Trials == false or not GetSeaBeastTrial();
					end;
				end;
			end;
		end);
	end;
end);

							repeat

								_tp(F.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 0, 15));
								sethiddenproperty(plr, "SimulationRadius", math.huge);
							until _G.Defeating == false or F.Humanoid.Health <= 0 or not F.Parent or not F:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") or not F:FindFirstChild("Humanoid");

function printBeltName(o)
	if type(o) == "table" and o.Quest.BeltName then
		return o.Quest.BeltName;
	end;
end;
spawn(function()
	while wait(Sec) do
		if _G.Dojoo then
			pcall(function()
				local o = { [1] = { NPC = "Dojo Trainer", Command = "RequestQuest" } };
				local F = (replicated.Modules.Net:FindFirstChild("RF/InteractDragonQuest")):InvokeServer(unpack(o));
				local J = printBeltName(F);
				if debug == false and (not F and not J) then
					_tp(CFrame.new(5865.0234375, 1208.3154296875, 871.15185546875));
					debug = true;
				elseif debug == true and ((CFrame.new(5865.0234375, 1208.3154296875, 871.15185546875)).Position - plr.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude <= 50 then
					if J == "White" then
						local o = GetConnectionEnemies("Skull Slayer");
						if o then
							repeat
								task.wait();
								A.Kill(o, _G.Dojoo);
							until not F or not _G.Dojoo or not A.Alive(o);
						else
							_tp(CFrame.new(-16759.58984375, 71.283767700195, 1595.3399658203));
						end;
					elseif J == "Yellow" then
						repeat
							task.wait();
							_G.SeaBeast1 = true;
							_G.TerrorShark = true;
							_G.Shark = true;
							_G.Piranha = true;
							_G.MobCrew = true;
							_G.FishBoat = true;
							_G.SailBoats = true;
						until not _G.Dojoo or not F;
						_G.SeaBeast1 = false;
						_G.TerrorShark = false;
						_G.Shark = false;
						_G.Piranha = false;
						_G.MobCrew = false;
						_G.FishBoat = false;
						_G.SailBoats = false;
					elseif J == "Green" then
						repeat
							task.wait();
							_G.SailBoats = true;
						until not _G.Dojoo or not F;
						_G.SailBoats = false;
					elseif J == "Purple" then
						repeat
							task.wait();
							_G.FarmEliteHunt = true;
						until not _G.Dojoo or not F;
						_G.FarmEliteHunt = false;
					elseif J == "Red" then
						repeat
							task.wait();
							_G.SailBoats = true;
							_G.FishBoat = true;
						until not _G.Dojoo or not F;
						_G.SailBoats = false;
						_G.FishBoat = false;
					elseif J == "Black" then
						repeat
							task.wait();
							if workspace.Map:FindFirstChild("PrehistoricIsland") or workspace._WorldOrigin.Locations:FindFirstChild("Prehistoric Island") then
								_G.Prehis_Find = true;
								if workspace.Map.PrehistoricIsland.Core.ActivationPrompt:FindFirstChild("ProximityPrompt", true) then
									_G.Prehis_Skills = false;
									_G.Prehis_Find = true;
								else
									_G.Prehis_Skills = true;
									_G.Prehis_Find = false;
								end;
							else
								_G.Prehis_Find = true;
								_G.Prehis_Skills = false;
							end;
						until not _G.Dojoo or not F;
						_G.Prehis_Find = false;
						_G.Prehis_Skills = false;
					elseif J == "Orange" or J == "Blue" then
						return nil;
					end;
				end;
				if not F then
					debug = false;
					local o = { [1] = { NPC = "Dojo Trainer", Command = "ClaimQuest" } };
					(replicated.Modules.Net:FindFirstChild("RF/InteractDragonQuest")):InvokeServer(unpack(o));
				end;
			end);
		end;
	end;
end);
BlazeEM = I.Prehistoric:AddToggle({
		Name = "Auto Dragon Hunter",
		Description = "",
		Default = false,
		Callback = function(o)
			_G.FarmBlazeEM = o;
		end,

checkQuesta = function()
		local o = { [1] = { Context = "Check" } };
		local F = nil;
		pcall(function()
			local o = { [1] = { Context = "RequestQuest" } };
			((((game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")):WaitForChild("Modules")):WaitForChild("Net")):WaitForChild("RF/DragonHunter")):InvokeServer(unpack(o));
		end);
		local J, D = pcall(function()
				F = ((((game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")):WaitForChild("Modules")):WaitForChild("Net")):WaitForChild("RF/DragonHunter")):InvokeServer(unpack(o));
			end);
		local G = false;
		local m;
		local X;
		local V;
		if F then
			if F.Text then
				G = true;
				local o = F.Text;
				if string.find(tostring(o), "Defeat") then
					V = 1;
					m = string.sub(tostring(o), 8, 9);
					m = tonumber(m);
					local F = { "Hydra Enforcer", "Venomous Assailant" };
					for F, J in pairs(F) do
						if string.find(o, J) then
							X = J;
							break;
						end;
					end;
				elseif string.find(tostring(o), "Destroy") then
					m = 10;
					V = 2;
					X = nil;
				end;
			end;
		end;
		return G, X, m, V;
	end;
BackTODoJo = function()
		for o, F in pairs((game:GetService("Players")).LocalPlayer.PlayerGui.Notifications:GetChildren()) do
			if F.Name == "NotificationTemplate" then
				if string.find(F.Text, "Head back to the Dojo to complete more tasks") then
					return true;
				end;
			end;
		end;
		return false;
	end;
DragonMobClear = function(o, F, J)
		if workspace.Enemies:FindFirstChild(F) then
			for J, D in pairs(workspace.Enemies:GetChildren()) do
				if D.Name == F and A.Alive(D) then
					if o then
						A.Kill(D, o);
					end;
				end;
			end;
		else
			_tp(J);
		end;
	end;
spawn(function()
	while wait() do
		if _G.FarmBlazeEM then
			pcall(function()
				local o, F, J, D = checkQuesta();
				if o == true and not BackTODoJo() then
					if D == 1 then
						if F == "Hydra Enforcer" or F == "Venomous Assailant" then
							repeat
								wait();
								DragonMobClear(true, F, CFrame.new(4620.6157226562, 1002.2954711914, 399.08688354492));
							until not _G.FarmBlazeEM or not o or BackTODoJo();
						end;
					elseif D == 2 then
						if workspace.Map.Waterfall.IslandModel:FindFirstChild("Meshes/bambootree", true) then
							repeat
								wait();
								spawn(function()
									_tp((workspace.Map.Waterfall.IslandModel:FindFirstChild("Meshes/bambootree", true)).CFrame * CFrame.new(4, 0, 0));
								end);
								if ((workspace.Map.Waterfall.IslandModel:FindFirstChild("Meshes/bambootree", true)).Position - Root.Position).Magnitude <= 200 then
									MousePos = (workspace.Map.Waterfall.IslandModel:FindFirstChild("Meshes/bambootree", true)).Position;
									Useskills("Melee", "Z");
									Useskills("Melee", "X");
									Useskills("Melee", "C");
									wait(.5);
									Useskills("Sword", "Z");
									Useskills("Sword", "X");
									wait(.5);
									Useskills("Blox Fruit", "Z");
									Useskills("Blox Fruit", "X");
									Useskills("Blox Fruit", "C");
									wait(.5);
									Useskills("Gun", "Z");
									Useskills("Gun", "X");
								end;
							until not _G.FarmBlazeEM or not o or BackTODoJo();
						end;
					end;
				else
					_tp(CFrame.new(5813, 1208, 884));
					DragonMobClear(false, nil, nil);
				end;
			end);
		end;
	end;
end);

	while wait(.1) do

					game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame = workspace.EmberTemplate.Part.CFrame;

				until not _G.AutoFireFlowers or not F.Parent or F.Humanoid.Health <= 0 or o;
			else
				_tp(CFrame.new(-13206.452148438, 425.89199829102, -7964.5537109375));
			end;
			if o then
				for o, F in pairs(o:GetChildren()) do

						local o = F.PrimaryPart.Position;
						local J = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position;
						local D = (o - J).Magnitude;

							vim1:SendKeyEvent(true, "E", false, game);
							wait(1.5);
							vim1:SendKeyEvent(false, "E", false, game);
						else
							_tp(CFrame.new(o));
						end;
					end;
				end;
			end;
		end;
	end;

I.Prehistoric:AddToggle({
	Name = "Auto Find Prehistoric Island",
	Description = "",
	Default = false,
	Callback = function(o)
		_G.Prehis_Find = o;
	end,
});
local k4 = nil;
spawn(function()
	while wait(Sec) do
		pcall(function()
			if _G.Prehis_Find then
				local o = plr.Character;
				if not o then
					return;
				end;
				local F = o:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart");
				local J = o:FindFirstChild("Humanoid");
				if not F or not J or J.Health <= 0 then
					return;
				end;
				local D = workspace._WorldOrigin.Locations;
				local G = D:FindFirstChild("Prehistoric Island", true);
				if not G then
					local o = CheckBoat();
					if not o then
						local o = CFrame.new(-16927.451, 9.086, 433.864);
						TeleportToTarget(o);
						if (o.Position - F.Position).Magnitude <= 10 then
							replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("BuyBoat", _G.SelectedBoat or "Guardian");
						end;
						return;
					end;
					if J.Sit == false then
						local F = o.VehicleSeat.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 1, 0);
						_tp(F);
						return;
					end;
					local D = CFrame.new(-10000000, 31, 37016.25);
					k4 = D;
					if CheckEnemiesBoat() or CheckTerrorShark() or CheckPirateGrandBrigade() then
						_tp(CFrame.new(-10000000, 150, 37016.25));
					else
						_tp(D);
					end;
				else
					local o = G:FindFirstChild("HeadTeleport", true) or G:FindFirstChild("Teleport_Head", true) or G:FindFirstChild("Head", true);
					if o then
						local J = o.CFrame;
						local D = (J.Position - J.LookVector * 40) + Vector3.new(0, 20, 0);
						if (D - F.Position).Magnitude > 30 then
							_tp(CFrame.new(D));
						end;
					else
						local o = G.CFrame.Position;
						local J = (o - F.Position).Unit;
						local D = (o - J * 250) + Vector3.new(0, 60, 0);
						_tp(CFrame.new(D));
					end;
				end;
			end;
		end);
	end;
end);
I.Prehistoric:AddToggle({ Name = "Auto Start Prehistoric Event", Default = false, Callback = function(o)
		_G.AutoStartPrehistoric = o;
	end });
spawn(function()
	while wait() do
		if _G.AutoStartPrehistoric then
			pcall(function()

				if o then
					if workspace.Map:FindFirstChild("PrehistoricIsland", true) then
						local o = workspace.Map.PrehistoricIsland.Core:FindFirstChild("ActivationPrompt", true);
						if o and o:FindFirstChild("ProximityPrompt") then
							if plr:DistanceFromCharacter(o.CFrame.Position) <= 150 then
								fireproximityprompt(o.ProximityPrompt, math.huge);
								vim1:SendKeyEvent(true, "E", false, game);
								wait(1.5);
								vim1:SendKeyEvent(false, "E", false, game);
							end;
							_tp(o.CFrame);
						end;
					end;
				end;
			end);
		end;
	end;
end);
I.Prehistoric:AddToggle({
	Name = "Auto Patch Prehistoric Event",
	Description = "",
	Default = false,
	Callback = function(o)
		_G.Prehis_Skills = o;
	end,
});
spawn(function()
	while wait(.3) do
		if _G.Prehis_Skills then
			pcall(function()
				local o = workspace.Map:FindFirstChild("PrehistoricIsland");
				if not o then
					return;
				end;
				for o, F in pairs(o:GetDescendants()) do
					if (F:IsA("BasePart") or F:IsA("MeshPart")) and (F.Name:lower()):find("lava") then
						F:Destroy();
					end;
				end;
				local F = o:FindFirstChild("Core");
				if F then
					local o = F:FindFirstChild("InteriorLava");
					if o then
						o:Destroy();
					end;
				end;
				local J = o:FindFirstChild("TrialTeleport");
				for o, F in pairs(o:GetDescendants()) do
					if F.Name == "TouchInterest" and not (J and F:IsDescendantOf(J)) then
						F.Parent:Destroy();
					end;
				end;
			end);
		end;
	end;
end);
spawn(function()
	while wait(Sec) do
		if _G.Prehis_Skills then
			pcall(function()
				local o = GetConnectionEnemies("Lava Golem");
				if o and o:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") then
					repeat
						wait(.1);
						A.Kill(o, true);
						o.Humanoid:ChangeState(15);
					until not _G.Prehis_Skills or not o.Parent or o.Humanoid.Health <= 0;
				end;
			end);
		end;
	end;
end);
spawn(function()
	while wait(Sec) do
		if _G.Prehis_Skills then
			pcall(function()
				local o = workspace.Map:FindFirstChild("PrehistoricIsland");
				if not o then
					return;
				end;
				local F = o:FindFirstChild("Core");
				if not F then
					return;
				end;
				local J = F:FindFirstChild("VolcanoRocks");
				if not J then
					return;
				end;
				for o, F in pairs(J:GetChildren()) do
					local J = F:FindFirstChild("VFXLayer");
					local D = J and J:FindFirstChild("At0");
					local G = D and D:FindFirstChild("Glow");
					if G and G.Enabled then
						repeat
							wait(.1);
							_tp(J.CFrame);
							if plr:DistanceFromCharacter(J.CFrame.Position) <= 150 then
								MousePos = J.CFrame.Position;
								Useskills("Melee", "Z");
								wait(.4);
								Useskills("Melee", "X");
								wait(.4);
								Useskills("Melee", "C");
								wait(.4);
								Useskills("Blox Fruit", "Z");
								wait(.4);
								Useskills("Blox Fruit", "X");
								wait(.4);
								Useskills("Blox Fruit", "C");
							end;
						until not _G.Prehis_Skills or not G.Enabled;
					end;
				end;
			end);
		end;
	end;
end);
Kaura = I.Prehistoric:AddToggle({
		Name = "Kill Aura",
		Description = "",
		Default = false,
		Callback = function(o)
			_G.KillAuraFull = o;
		end,
	});
local n4 = 500;
local M4 = 2;
spawn(function()
	while task.wait(M4) do
		if _G.KillAuraFull then
			pcall(function()
				local o = game.Players.LocalPlayer;
				local F = o.Character;
				local J = F and F:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart");
				if not J then
					return;
				end;
				sethiddenproperty(o, "SimulationRadius", math.huge);
				for o, F in pairs(workspace.Enemies:GetChildren()) do
					if F:FindFirstChild("Humanoid") and F:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") then
						local o = (F.HumanoidRootPart.Position - J.Position).Magnitude;
						if o <= n4 and F.Humanoid.Health > 0 then
							F.Humanoid.Health = 0;
							F.HumanoidRootPart.CanCollide = false;
							F:BreakJoints();
						end;
					end;
				end;
			end);
		end;
	end;
end);

				end;
			end;
		end;
	end;

I.SeaEvent:AddSection("Choose Sea Event");
Q = I.SeaEvent:AddDropdown({ Name = "Select Boats", Options = p4, Callback = function(o)
			_G.SelectedBoat = o;
		end });
I.SeaEvent:AddButton({ Name = "Buy Boats", Description = "", Callback = function()
		replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("BuyBoat", _G.SelectedBoat);
	end });
Q = I.SeaEvent:AddDropdown({ Name = "Select Sea Level", Options = K4, Callback = function(o)
			_G.DangerSc = o;
		end });
Q = I.SeaEvent:AddToggle({
		Name = "Auto Sail Boat",
		Description = "",
		Default = false,
		Callback = function(o)
			_G.SailBoats = o;
		end,
	});
spawn(function()
	while wait() do
		if _G.SailBoats then
			pcall(function()
				local o = CheckBoat();
				if not o and (not (CheckShark() and _G.Shark or CheckTerrorShark() and _G.TerrorShark or CheckFishCrew() and _G.MobCrew or CheckPiranha() and _G.Piranha) and (not (CheckEnemiesBoat() and _G.FishBoat) and (not (CheckSeaBeast() and _G.SeaBeast1) and (not (_G.PGB and CheckPirateGrandBrigade()) and (not (_G.HCM and CheckHauntedCrew()) and not (_G.Leviathan1 and CheckLeviathan())))))) then
					local o = CFrame.new(-16927.451, 9.086, 433.864);
					TeleportToTarget(o);
					if (o.Position - plr.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude <= 10 then
						replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("BuyBoat", _G.SelectedBoat);
					end;
				elseif o and (not (CheckShark() and _G.Shark or CheckTerrorShark() and _G.TerrorShark or CheckFishCrew() and _G.MobCrew or CheckPiranha() and _G.Piranha) and (not (CheckEnemiesBoat() and _G.FishBoat) and (not (CheckSeaBeast() and _G.SeaBeast1) and (not (_G.PGB and CheckPirateGrandBrigade()) and (not (_G.HCM and CheckHauntedCrew()) and not (_G.Leviathan1 and CheckLeviathan())))))) then
					if plr.Character.Humanoid.Sit == false then
						local F = o.VehicleSeat.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 1, 0);
						_tp(F);
					else
						if _G.DangerSc == "Lv 1" then
							CFrameSelectedZone = CFrame.new(-21998.375, 30.0006084, -682.309143);
						elseif _G.DangerSc == "Lv 2" then
							CFrameSelectedZone = CFrame.new(-26779.5215, 30.0005474, -822.858032);
						elseif _G.DangerSc == "Lv 3" then
							CFrameSelectedZone = CFrame.new(-31171.957, 30.0001011, -2256.93774);
						elseif _G.DangerSc == "Lv 4" then
							CFrameSelectedZone = CFrame.new(-34054.6875, 30.2187767, -2560.12012);
						elseif _G.DangerSc == "Lv 5" then
							CFrameSelectedZone = CFrame.new(-38887.5547, 30.0004578, -2162.99023);
						elseif _G.DangerSc == "Lv 6" then
							CFrameSelectedZone = CFrame.new(-44541.7617, 30.0003204, -1244.8584);
						elseif _G.DangerSc == "Lv Infinite" then
							CFrameSelectedZone = CFrame.new(-10000000, 31, 37016.25);
						end;
						repeat
							wait();
							if not _G.FishBoat and CheckEnemiesBoat() or not _G.PGB and CheckPirateGrandBrigade() or not _G.TerrorShark and CheckTerrorShark() then
								_tp(CFrameSelectedZone * CFrame.new(0, 150, 0));
							else
								_tp(CFrameSelectedZone);
							end;
						until _G.SailBoats == false or CheckShark() and _G.Shark or CheckTerrorShark() and _G.TerrorShark or CheckFishCrew() and _G.MobCrew or CheckPiranha() and _G.Piranha or CheckSeaBeast() and _G.SeaBeast1 or CheckEnemiesBoat() and _G.FishBoat or _G.Leviathan1 and CheckLeviathan() or _G.HCM and CheckHauntedCrew() or _G.PGB and CheckPirateGrandBrigade() or (plr.Character:WaitForChild("Humanoid")).Sit == false;
						plr.Character.Humanoid.Sit = false;
					end;
				end;
			end);
		end;
	end;
end);
spawn(function()
	while wait(Sec) do
		pcall(function()
			for o, F in pairs(workspace.Boats:GetChildren()) do
				for o, F in pairs(workspace.Boats[F.Name]:GetDescendants()) do
					if F:IsA("BasePart") then
						if _G.SailBoats or _G.Prehis_Find or _G.FindMirage or _G.SailBoat_Hydra or _G.AutofindKitIs then
							F.CanCollide = false;
						else
							F.CanCollide = true;
						end;
					end;
				end;
			end;
		end);
	end;
end);

I.SeaEvent:AddToggle({
	Name = "Auto Attack Sea Beast",
	Description = "",
	Default = false,
	Callback = function(o)
		_G.SeaBeast1 = o;
	end,
});
spawn(function()
	while wait() do
		pcall(function()
			if _G.Shark then
				local o = { "Shark" };
				if CheckShark() then
					for F, J in pairs(workspace.Enemies:GetChildren()) do
						if table.find(o, J.Name) then
							if A.Alive(J) then
								repeat
									task.wait();
									A.Kill(J, _G.Shark);
								until _G.Shark == false or not J.Parent or J.Humanoid.Health <= 0;
							end;
						end;
					end;
				end;
			end;
			if _G.TerrorShark then
				local o = { "Terrorshark" };
				if CheckTerrorShark() then
					for F, J in pairs(workspace.Enemies:GetChildren()) do
						if table.find(o, J.Name) then
							if A.Alive(J) then
								repeat
									task.wait();
									A.KillSea(J, _G.TerrorShark);
								until _G.TerrorShark == false or not J.Parent or J.Humanoid.Health <= 0;
							end;
						end;
					end;
				end;
			end;
			if _G.Piranha then
				local o = { "Piranha" };
				if CheckPiranha() then
					for F, J in pairs(workspace.Enemies:GetChildren()) do
						if table.find(o, J.Name) then
							if A.Alive(J) then
								repeat
									task.wait();
									A.Kill(J, _G.Piranha);
								until _G.Piranha == false or not J.Parent or J.Humanoid.Health <= 0;
							end;
						end;
					end;
				end;
			end;
			if _G.MobCrew then
				local o = { "Fish Crew Member" };
				if CheckFishCrew() then
					for F, J in pairs(workspace.Enemies:GetChildren()) do
						if table.find(o, J.Name) then
							if A.Alive(J) then
								repeat
									task.wait();
									A.Kill(J, _G.MobCrew);
								until _G.MobCrew == false or not J.Parent or J.Humanoid.Health <= 0;
							end;
						end;
					end;
				end;
			end;
			if _G.HCM then
				local o = { "Haunted Crew Member" };
				if CheckHauntedCrew() then
					for F, J in pairs(workspace.Enemies:GetChildren()) do
						if table.find(o, J.Name) then
							if A.Alive(J) then
								repeat
									task.wait();
									A.Kill(J, _G.HCM);
								until _G.HCM == false or not J.Parent or J.Humanoid.Health <= 0;
							end;
						end;
					end;
				end;
			end;
			if _G.SeaBeast1 then
				if workspace.SeaBeasts:FindFirstChild("SeaBeast1") then
					for o, F in pairs(workspace.SeaBeasts:GetChildren()) do
						if F:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") and (F:FindFirstChild("Health") and F.Health.Value > 0) then
							repeat
								task.wait();
								spawn(function()
									_tp(CFrame.new(F.HumanoidRootPart.Position.X, (game:GetService("Workspace")).Map["WaterBase-Plane"].Position.Y + 200, F.HumanoidRootPart.Position.Z));
								end);
								if plr:DistanceFromCharacter(F.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame.Position) <= 500 then
									AitSeaSkill_Custom = F.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame;
									MousePos = AitSeaSkill_Custom.Position;
									if CheckF() then
										weaponSc("Blox Fruit");
										Useskills("Blox Fruit", "Z");
										Useskills("Blox Fruit", "X");
										Useskills("Blox Fruit", "C");
									else
										Useskills("Melee", "Z");
										Useskills("Melee", "X");
										Useskills("Melee", "C");
										wait(.1);
										Useskills("Sword", "Z");
										Useskills("Sword", "X");
										wait(.1);
										Useskills("Blox Fruit", "Z");
										Useskills("Blox Fruit", "X");
										Useskills("Blox Fruit", "C");
										wait(.1);
										Useskills("Gun", "Z");
										Useskills("Gun", "X");
									end;
								end;
							until _G.SeaBeast1 == false or not F:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") or not F.Parent or F.Health.Value <= 0;
						end;
					end;
				end;
			end;
			if _G.Leviathan1 then
				if workspace.SeaBeasts:FindFirstChild("Leviathan") then
					for o, F in pairs(workspace.SeaBeasts:GetChildren()) do
						if F:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") and (F:FindFirstChild("Leviathan Segment") and (F:FindFirstChild("Health") and F.Health.Value > 0)) then
							repeat
								task.wait();
								spawn(function()
									_tp(CFrame.new(F.HumanoidRootPart.Position.X, (game:GetService("Workspace")).Map["WaterBase-Plane"].Position.Y + 200, F.HumanoidRootPart.Position.Z));
								end);
								if plr:DistanceFromCharacter(F.HumanoidRootPart.CFrame.Position) <= 500 then
									MousePos = (F:FindFirstChild("Leviathan Segment")).Position;
									if CheckF() then
										weaponSc("Blox Fruit");
										Useskills("Blox Fruit", "Z");
										Useskills("Blox Fruit", "X");
										Useskills("Blox Fruit", "C");
									else
										Useskills("Melee", "Z");
										Useskills("Melee", "X");
										Useskills("Melee", "C");
										wait(.1);
										Useskills("Sword", "Z");
										Useskills("Sword", "X");
										wait(.1);
										Useskills("Blox Fruit", "Z");
										Useskills("Blox Fruit", "X");
										Useskills("Blox Fruit", "C");
										wait(.1);
										Useskills("Gun", "Z");
										Useskills("Gun", "X");
									end;
								end;
							until _G.Leviathan1 == false or not F:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") or not F.Parent or F.Health.Value <= 0;
						end;
					end;
				end;
			end;
			if _G.FishBoat then
				if CheckEnemiesBoat() then
					for o, F in pairs(workspace.Enemies:GetChildren()) do
						if F:FindFirstChild("Health") and (F.Health.Value > 0 and F:FindFirstChild("VehicleSeat")) then
							repeat
								task.wait();
								spawn(function()
									if F.Name == "FishBoat" then
										_tp(F.Engine.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, -50, -25));
									end;
								end);
								if plr:DistanceFromCharacter(F.Engine.CFrame.Position) <= 150 then
									AitSeaSkill_Custom = F.Engine.CFrame;
									MousePos = AitSeaSkill_Custom.Position;
									if CheckF() then
										weaponSc("Blox Fruit");
										Useskills("Blox Fruit", "Z");
										Useskills("Blox Fruit", "X");
										Useskills("Blox Fruit", "C");
									else
										Useskills("Melee", "Z");
										Useskills("Melee", "X");
										Useskills("Melee", "C");
										wait(.1);
										Useskills("Sword", "Z");
										Useskills("Sword", "X");
										wait(.1);
										Useskills("Blox Fruit", "Z");
										Useskills("Blox Fruit", "X");
										Useskills("Blox Fruit", "C");
										wait(.1);
										Useskills("Gun", "Z");
										Useskills("Gun", "X");
									end;
								end;
							until _G.FishBoat == false or not F:FindFirstChild("VehicleSeat") or F.Health.Value <= 0;
						end;
					end;
				end;
			end;
			if _G.PGB then
				if CheckPirateGrandBrigade() then
					for o, F in pairs(workspace.Enemies:GetChildren()) do
						if F:FindFirstChild("Health") and (F.Health.Value > 0 and F:FindFirstChild("VehicleSeat")) then
							repeat
								task.wait();
								spawn(function()
									if F.Name == "PirateBrigade" then
										_tp(F.Engine.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, -30, -10));
									elseif F.Name == "PirateGrandBrigade" then
										_tp(F.Engine.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, -50, -50));
									end;
								end);
								if plr:DistanceFromCharacter(F.Engine.CFrame.Position) <= 150 then
									AitSeaSkill_Custom = F.Engine.CFrame;
									MousePos = AitSeaSkill_Custom.Position;
									if CheckF() then
										weaponSc("Blox Fruit");
										Useskills("Blox Fruit", "Z");
										Useskills("Blox Fruit", "X");
										Useskills("Blox Fruit", "C");
									else
										Useskills("Melee", "Z");
										Useskills("Melee", "X");
										Useskills("Melee", "C");
										wait(.1);
										Useskills("Sword", "Z");
										Useskills("Sword", "X");
										wait(.1);
										Useskills("Blox Fruit", "Z");
										Useskills("Blox Fruit", "X");
										Useskills("Blox Fruit", "C");
										wait(.1);
										Useskills("Gun", "Z");
										Useskills("Gun", "X");
									end;
								end;
							until _G.PGB == false or not F:FindFirstChild("VehicleSeat") or F.Health.Value <= 0;
						end;
					end;
				end;
			end;
		end);
	end;
end);
I.SeaEvent:AddSection("Kitsune Island / Event");
local ok = I.SeaEvent:AddParagraph("Kitsune Island Status", "");
spawn(function()
	while wait(.2) do
		if workspace.Map:FindFirstChild("KitsuneIsland") or workspace._WorldOrigin.Locations:FindFirstChild("Kitsune Island") then
			ok:SetDesc("Kitsune Island : True");
		else
			ok:SetDesc("Kitsune Island : False");
		end;
	end;
end);
I.SeaEvent:AddToggle({
	Name = "Auto Find Kitsune Island",
	Description = "",
	Default = false,
	Callback = function(o)
		_G.AutofindKitIs = o;
	end,
});
spawn(function()
	while wait() do
		if _G.AutofindKitIs then
			pcall(function()
				if not workspace._WorldOrigin.Locations:FindFirstChild("Kitsune Island", true) then
					local o = CheckBoat();
					if not o then
						local o = CFrame.new(-16927.451, 9.086, 433.864);
						TeleportToTarget(o);
						if (o.Position - plr.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude <= 10 then
							replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("BuyBoat", _G.SelectedBoat);
						end;
					else
						if plr.Character.Humanoid.Sit == false then
							local F = o.VehicleSeat.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 1, 0);
							_tp(F);
						else
							local o = CFrame.new(-10000000, 31, 37016.25);
							repeat
								wait();
								if CheckEnemiesBoat() or CheckTerrorShark() or CheckPirateGrandBrigade() then
									_tp(CFrame.new(-10000000, 150, 37016.25));
								else
									_tp(CFrame.new(-10000000, 31, 37016.25));
								end;
							until not _G.AutofindKitIs or (o.Position - plr.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude <= 10 or workspace._WorldOrigin.Locations:FindFirstChild("Kitsune Island") or plr.Character.Humanoid.Sit == false;
							plr.Character.Humanoid.Sit = false;
						end;
					end;
				else
					_tp((workspace._WorldOrigin.Locations:FindFirstChild("Kitsune Island")).CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 500, 0));
				end;
			end);
		end;
	end;
end);
I.SeaEvent:AddToggle({
	Name = "Auto Teleport to Shrine Actived",
	Description = "",
	Default = false,
	Callback = function(o)
		_G.tweenShrine = o;
	end,
});
spawn(function()
	while wait(.1) do
		if _G.tweenShrine then
			pcall(function()
				local o = workspace.Map:FindFirstChild("KitsuneIsland") or game.Workspace._WorldOrigin.Locations:FindFirstChild("Kitsune Island");
				local F = o:FindFirstChild("ShrineActive");
				if F then
					for F, J in next, F:GetDescendants() do
						if J:IsA("BasePart") and J.Name:find("NeonShrinePart") then
							(replicated.Modules.Net:FindFirstChild("RE/TouchKitsuneStatue")):FireServer();
							repeat
								wait();
								_tp(J.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 2, 0));
							until _G.tweenShrine == false or not o;
						end;
					end;
				else
					_tp((workspace._WorldOrigin.Locations:FindFirstChild("Kitsune Island")).CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 500, 0));
				end;
			end);
		end;
	end;
end);

				end;
			end);
		end;
	end;
end);

local Jk = I.SeaEvent:AddParagraph("Spy Status", "");
spawn(function()
	while wait(.2) do
		pcall(function()
			local o = string.match(replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("InfoLeviathan", "1"), "%d+");
			if o then
				Jk:SetDesc("Spy Leviathan : " .. tostring(o));
				if tonumber(o) == 5 then
					Jk:SetDesc("Spy Leviathan : Already Done!!");
				end;
			end;
		end);
	end;
end);
I.SeaEvent:AddButton({ Name = "Buy Spy", Callback = function()
		(game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")).Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("InfoLeviathan", "2");
	end });
I.SeaEvent:AddToggle({
	Name = "Auto Teleport Frozen Dimension",
	Description = "",
	Default = false,
	Callback = function(o)

	end,
});
spawn(function()
	while wait(.1) do
		if _G.FrozenTP then
			pcall(function()
				if workspace.Map:FindFirstChild("LeviathanGate") then
					_tp(workspace.Map.LeviathanGate.CFrame);
					((replicated:WaitForChild("Remotes")):WaitForChild("CommF_")):InvokeServer("OpenLeviathanGate");
				end;
			end);

I.SeaEvent:AddToggle({
	Name = "Auto Drive To Hydra Island",
	Description = "",
	Default = false,
	Callback = function(o)
		_G.SailBoat_Hydra = o;
	end,
});
spawn(function()
	while wait() do
		if _G.SailBoat_Hydra then
			pcall(function()
				local o = CheckBoat();
				if not o then
					local o = CFrame.new(-16927.451, 9.086, 433.864);
					TeleportToTarget(o);
					if (o.Position - plr.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude <= 10 then
						replicated.Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("BuyBoat", _G.SelectedBoat);
					end;
				elseif o then
					if plr.Character.Humanoid.Sit == false then
						local F = o.VehicleSeat.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 1, 0);
						_tp(F);
					else
						repeat
							wait();
							if CheckEnemiesBoat() or CheckPirateGrandBrigade() or CheckTerrorShark() then
								_tp(CFrame.new(5433, 150, 290));
							else
								_tp(CFrame.new(5433, 35, 290));
							end;
						until _G.SailBoat_Hydra == false or (plr.Character:WaitForChild("Humanoid")).Sit == false;
						plr.Character.Humanoid.Sit = false;
					end;
				end;
			end);
		end;
	end;
end);

I.Esp:AddSection("Esp");
function isnil(o)
	return o == nil;
end;
local function Dk(o)
	return math.floor(tonumber(o) + .5);
end;
Number = math.random(1, 1000000);
local Gk = (game:GetService("Players")).LocalPlayer;
local mk = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage");
local Xk = Gk.Team;
EspPly = function()
		for o, F in next, game.Players:GetChildren() do
			pcall(function()
				if not isnil(F.Character) then
					if PlayerEsp then
						if not isnil(F.Character.Head) and not F.Character.Head:FindFirstChild("NameEsp" .. Number) then
							local o = Instance.new("BillboardGui", F.Character.Head);
							o.Name = "NameEsp" .. Number;
							o.ExtentsOffset = Vector3.new(0, 1, 0);
							o.Size = UDim2.new(1, 200, 1, 30);
							o.Adornee = F.Character.Head;
							o.AlwaysOnTop = true;
							local J = Instance.new("TextLabel", o);
							J.Font = Enum.Font.Code;
							J.FontSize = "Size14";
							J.TextWrapped = true;
							J.Text = F.Name .. (" \n" .. (Dk((Gk.Character.Head.Position - F.Character.Head.Position).Magnitude / 3) .. " M"));
							J.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0);
							J.TextYAlignment = "Top";
							J.BackgroundTransparency = 1;
							J.TextStrokeTransparency = .5;
							if F.Team == Xk then
								J.TextColor3 = Color3.new(0, 0, 254);
							else
								J.TextColor3 = Color3.new(255, 0, 0);
							end;
						else
							if F.Character.Head:FindFirstChild("NameEsp" .. Number) then
								F.Character.Head["NameEsp" .. Number].TextLabel.Text = F.Name .. (" | " .. (Dk((Gk.Character.Head.Position - F.Character.Head.Position).Magnitude / 3) .. (" M\nHealth : " .. (Dk((F.Character.Humanoid.Health * 100) / F.Character.Humanoid.MaxHealth) .. "%"))));
							end;
						end;
					else
						if F.Character.Head:FindFirstChild("NameEsp" .. Number) then
							(F.Character.Head:FindFirstChild("NameEsp" .. Number)):Destroy();
						end;
					end;
				end;
			end);
		end;
	end;

	end;

ChestEsp = function()
		if ChestESP then
			local o = game:GetService("CollectionService");
			local F = o:GetTagged("_ChestTagged");
			for o, F in ipairs(F) do
				pcall(function()
					local o = (F:GetPivot()).Position;
					local J = (o - Gk.Character.Head.Position).Magnitude;
					local D = (F:GetFullName()):gsub("[^%w_]", "_");
					local G = F:FindFirstChild("ChestEspAttachment");
					if not G then
						local o = Instance.new("Attachment");
						o.Name = "ChestEspAttachment";
						o.Parent = F;
						o.Position = Vector3.new(0, 3, 0);
						local J = Instance.new("BillboardGui");
						J.Name = "NameEsp";
						J.Size = UDim2.new(0, 200, 0, 30);
						J.Adornee = o;
						J.ExtentsOffset = Vector3.new(0, 1, 0);
						J.AlwaysOnTop = true;
						J.Parent = o;
						local D = Instance.new("TextLabel");
						D.Font = Enum.Font.Code;
						D.TextSize = 14;
						D.TextWrapped = true;
						D.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0);
						D.TextYAlignment = Enum.TextYAlignment.Top;
						D.BackgroundTransparency = 1;
						D.TextStrokeTransparency = .5;
						D.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(80, 245, 245);
						D.Parent = J;
					end;
					local m = G and G:FindFirstChild("NameEsp");
					if m then
						local o = math.floor(J / 3);
						local D = F.Name:gsub("Label", "");
						m.TextLabel.Text = string.format("[%s] %d M", D, o);
					end;
				end);
			end;
		else
			for o, F in ipairs((game:GetService("CollectionService")):GetTagged("_ChestTagged")) do
				local J = F:FindFirstChild("ChestEspAttachment");
				if J then
					J:Destroy();
				end;
			end;
		end;
	end;
berriesEsp = function()
		if BerryEsp then
			local o = game:GetService("CollectionService");
			local F = o:GetTagged("BerryBush");
			for o, F in ipairs(F) do
				pcall(function()
					local o = (F.Parent:GetPivot()).Position;
					for F, J in pairs(F:GetAttributes()) do
						if J then
							local F = "BerryEspPart_" .. (J .. ("_" .. tostring(o)));
							local D = workspace:FindFirstChild(F);
							if not D then
								D = Instance.new("Part");
								D.Name = F;
								D.Transparency = 1;
								D.Size = Vector3.new(1, 1, 1);
								D.Anchored = true;
								D.CanCollide = false;
								D.Parent = workspace;
								D.CFrame = CFrame.new(o);
							end;
							if not D:FindFirstChild("NameEsp") then
								local o = Instance.new("BillboardGui", D);
								o.Name = "NameEsp";
								o.ExtentsOffset = Vector3.new(0, 1, 0);
								o.Size = UDim2.new(0, 200, 0, 30);
								o.Adornee = D;
								o.AlwaysOnTop = true;
								local F = Instance.new("TextLabel", o);
								F.Font = Enum.Font.Code;
								F.TextSize = 14;
								F.TextWrapped = true;
								F.Size = UDim2.new(1, 0, 1, 0);
								F.TextYAlignment = Enum.TextYAlignment.Top;
								F.BackgroundTransparency = 1;
								F.TextStrokeTransparency = .5;
								F.TextColor3 = Color3.fromRGB(80, 245, 245);
							end;
							local G = D:FindFirstChild("NameEsp");
							local m = (Gk.Character.Head.Position - o).Magnitude / 3;
							if G then
								G.TextLabel.Text = "[" .. (J .. ("]" .. (" " .. (math.round(m) .. " M"))));
							end;
						end;
					end;
				end);
			end;
		else
			for o, F in ipairs(workspace:GetChildren()) do
				if F:IsA("Part") and F.Name:match("BerryEspPart_.*") then
					F:Destroy();
				end;
			end;
		end;
	end;
I.Esp:AddToggle({
	Name = "Esp Berry",
	Description = "",
	Default = false,
	Callback = function(o)
		BerryEsp = o;
		if not o then
			for o, F in ipairs(workspace:GetChildren()) do
				if F:IsA("Part") and F.Name:match("BerryEspPart_.*") then
					F:Destroy();
				end;
			end;
		else
			task.spawn(function()
				while BerryEsp do
					berriesEsp();
					task.wait();
				end;
			end);
		end;
	end,
});
I.Esp:AddToggle({
	Name = "Esp Player",
	Description = "",
	Default = false,
	Callback = function(o)
		PlayerEsp = o;
		if not o then
			for o, F in next, game.Players:GetChildren() do
				pcall(function()
					if not isnil(F.Character) and not isnil(F.Character.Head) then
						if F.Character.Head:FindFirstChild("NameEsp" .. Number) then
							(F.Character.Head:FindFirstChild("NameEsp" .. Number)):Destroy();
						end;
					end;
				end);
			end;
		else
			task.spawn(function()
				while PlayerEsp do
					EspPly();
					task.wait();
				end;
			end);
		end;
	end,
});
I.Esp:AddToggle({
	Name = "Esp Chest",
	Description = "",
	Default = false,
	Callback = function(o)
		ChestESP = o;
		if not o then
			for o, F in ipairs((game:GetService("CollectionService")):GetTagged("_ChestTagged")) do
				local J = F:FindFirstChild("ChestEspAttachment");
				if J then
					J:Destroy();
				end;
			end;
		else
			task.spawn(function()
				while ChestESP do
					ChestEsp();
					task.wait();
				end;
			end);
		end;

I.Raids:AddSection("Fruits Options");
local function Vk(o)
	local F = tostring(o);
	repeat
		local o, J = F:gsub("^(-?%d+)(%d%d%d)", "%1,%2");
		F = o;
	until J == 0;
	return F;
end;
local function jk()
	local o = "Advance Fruit Stock\n";
	local F, J = pcall(function()
			return (game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")).Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("GetFruits", true);
		end);
	if not F or not J then
		o = o .. "- Error while retrieving data.\n";
	else
		local F = false;
		for J, D in pairs(J) do
			if D.OnSale then
				F = true;
				o = o .. (D.Name .. (" - $" .. (Vk(D.Price) .. "\n")));
			end;
		end;
		if not F then
			o = o .. "- No fruit.\n";
		end;
	end;
	o = o .. "\nNormal Fruit Stock\n";
	local D, G = pcall(function()
			return (game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage")).Remotes.CommF_:InvokeServer("GetFruits");
		end);
	if D and G then
		local F = false;
		for J, D in pairs(G) do
			if D.OnSale then
				F = true;
				o = o .. (D.Name .. (" - $" .. (Vk(D.Price) .. "\n")));
			end;
		end;
		if not F then
			o = o .. "- No fruit.\n";
		end;
	else
		o = o .. "- Error while retrieving data.\n";
	end;
	return o;
end;
local Yk = I.Raids:AddParagraph("Stock Fruit", "Loading...");
task.spawn(function()
	while task.wait(60) do
		pcall(function()
			Yk:SetDesc(jk());
		end);
	end;
end);
pcall(function()
	Yk:SetDesc(jk());
end);

						fireclickdetector(o.ClickDetector);
					end;
				end;
			end;
			if World3 then
				local o = workspace.Map["Boat Castle"].RaidSummon2.Button.Main;
				if o then
					if o:FindFirstChild("ProximityPrompt") then
						fireproximityprompt(o.ProximityPrompt);
					elseif o:FindFirstChild("ClickDetector") then
						fireclickdetector(o.ClickDetector);
					end;
				end;
			end;
		end);
	end;
end);
Raiding = I.Raids:AddToggle({
		Name = "Auto Raid + Next Island",
		Description = "",
		Default = false,
		Callback = function(o)
			_G.Raiding = o;
		end,
	});
spawn(function()
	local o = workspace._WorldOrigin.Locations;
	local F = {
			"Island 1",
			"Island 2",
			"Island 3",
			"Island 4",
			"Island 5",
		};
	local J = nil;
	while task.wait(.3) do
		if not _G.Raiding then
			continue;
		end;
		local D = Gk.PlayerGui.Main.TopHUDList.RaidTimer;
		if not D.Visible then
			continue;
		end;
		local G = Gk.Character;
		if not G then
			continue;
		end;
		local m = G:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart");
		local X = G:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid");
		if not m or not X or X.Health <= 0 then
			continue;
		end;
		if X.Sit or X.PlatformStand or m.Anchored then
			continue;
		end;
		local V = 999999;
		for F, D in ipairs(F) do
			local G = o:FindFirstChild(D);
			if G then
				local o = (m.Position - G.Position).Magnitude;
				if o < V then
					V = o;
					J = D;
				end;
			end;
		end;
		if not J then
			continue;
		end;
		local j = o:FindFirstChild(J);
		if not j then
			continue;
		end;
		local Y = false;
		for o, F in ipairs(workspace.Enemies:GetChildren()) do
			local J = F:FindFirstChild("Humanoid");
			local D = F:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart");
			if J and (D and J.Health > 0) then
				if (D.Position - j.Position).Magnitude < 450 then
					Y = true;
					repeat
						task.wait();
						A.Kill(F, _G.Raiding);
					until not _G.Raiding or not F.Parent or J.Health <= 0;
				end;
			end;
		end;
		if not Y then
			local D = table.find(F, J);
			if D and F[D + 1] then
				local G = o:FindFirstChild(F[D + 1]);
				if G then
					local o = G.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 45, 120);
					_tp(o);
				end;
				J = F[D + 1];
				task.wait(1);
			end;
		end;
	end;
end);

I.Raids:AddToggle({
	Name = "Auto Farm Dungeon",
	Description = "",
	Default = false,
	Callback = function(o)
		_G.AutoFarmDungeon = o;
	end,
});
local Ak = 5000;
spawn(function()
	while task.wait(.15) do
		if not _G.AutoFarmDungeon then
			continue;
		end;
		pcall(function()
			local o = game.Players.LocalPlayer;
			local F = o.Character;
			local J = F and F:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart");
			local D = F and F:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid");
			if not J or not D or D.Health <= 0 then
				return;
			end;
			for o, F in pairs(workspace.Enemies:GetChildren()) do
				if not _G.AutoFarmDungeon then
					break;
				end;
				local D = F:FindFirstChild("Humanoid");
				local G = F:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart");
				if D and (G and D.Health > 0) then
					local o = (G.Position - J.Position).Magnitude;
					if o <= Ak then
						repeat
							task.wait();
							A.Kill(F, true);
						until not _G.AutoFarmDungeon or not F.Parent or D.Health <= 0;
					end;
				end;
			end;
		end);
	end;
end);
I.Raids:AddToggle({ Name = "TP Exit (1)", Default = false, Callback = function(o)
		_G.TPFloor1 = o;
	end });
local gk = false;
local function lk()
	local o = rk();
	if not o then
		return;
	end;
	for F, J in pairs(workspace.Map.Dungeon:GetChildren()) do
		local D = J:FindFirstChild("ExitTeleporter");
		if D and D:FindFirstChild("Root") then
			if (o.Position - D.Root.Position).Magnitude < 200 then
				return D.Root;
			end;
		end;
	end;
end;
task.spawn(function()
	while task.wait(.3) do
		if not _G.TPFloor1 then
			gk = false;
			continue;
		end;
		if not gk then
			local o = lk();
			if o then
				o = o.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 3, 0);
				(rk()).CFrame = o;
				gk = true;
			end;
		end;
	end;
end);
I.Raids:AddToggle({ Name = "TP Exit (2)", Default = false, Callback = function(o)
		_G.TPFloor2 = o;
	end });
local Zk = false;
task.spawn(function()
	while task.wait(.3) do
		if not _G.TPFloor2 then
			Zk = false;
			continue;
		end;
		if Zk then
			continue;
		end;
		local o = rk();
		if not o then
			continue;
		end;
		for F, J in pairs(workspace.Map.Dungeon:GetChildren()) do
			local D = J:FindFirstChild("EntranceTeleporter");
			local G = J:FindFirstChild("ExitTeleporter");
			if D and (G and (D:FindFirstChild("Root") and G:FindFirstChild("Root"))) then
				if (o.Position - D.Root.Position).Magnitude < 100 then
					o.CFrame = G.Root.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 3, 0);
					Zk = true;
					break;
				end;
			end;
		end;
	end;
end);

		_G.TPFloor3 = o;
	end });
local vk = false;
local function Wk()
	local o;
	for F, J in pairs(workspace.Map.Dungeon:GetChildren()) do
		local D = tonumber(J.Name);
		if D and (not o or D > tonumber(o.Name)) then
			o = J;
		end;
	end;
	return o;
end;
task.spawn(function()
	while task.wait(.3) do
		if not _G.TPFloor3 then
			vk = false;
			continue;
		end;
		if not vk then
			local o = Wk();
			if o and (o:FindFirstChild("ExitTeleporter") and o.ExitTeleporter:FindFirstChild("Root")) then
				(rk()).CFrame = o.ExitTeleporter.Root.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 3, 0);
				vk = true;
			end;
		end;
	end;
end);
I.Raids:AddToggle({ Name = "TP Exit (4)", Default = false, Callback = function(o)
		_G.TPFloor4 = o;
	end });
local sk = false;
local function Sk()
	local o = rk();
	if not o then
		return;
	end;
	local F, J = nil, math.huge;
	for D, G in pairs(workspace.Map.Dungeon:GetChildren()) do
		local m = G:FindFirstChild("ExitTeleporter");
		if m and m:FindFirstChild("Root") then
			local D = (o.Position - m.Root.Position).Magnitude;
			if D < J then
				J = D;
				F = m.Root;
			end;
		end;
	end;
	return F;
end;
task.spawn(function()
	while task.wait(.3) do
		if not _G.TPFloor4 then
			sk = false;
			continue;
		end;
		if not sk then
			local o = Sk();
			if o then
				(rk()).CFrame = o.CFrame * CFrame.new(0, 3, 0);
				sk = true;
			end;
		end;
	end;
end);

						for J, D in next, ply:GetPlayers() do
							if D ~= Bk then
								if D.Character and (D.Character:FindFirstChild("Head") and (_G.AimCam and D.Character.Humanoid.Health > 0)) then

										F = D;
									end;
								end;
							end;
						end;
						return F;
					end;
				repeat
					task.wait();
					o.CFrame = CFrame.new(o.CFrame.Position, (closestplayer()).Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position);
				until _G.AimCam == false or Mag > dist;
			end;
		end);

							(game:GetService("VirtualUser")):CaptureController();
							(game:GetService("VirtualUser")):Button1Down(Vector2.new(1280, 672));
						until _G.AutoPlayerHunter == false or F.Humanoid.Health <= 0;
						Useskill = false;

					end;
				end;
			end;
		end;
	end;
end);

I.Combat:AddSection("LocalPlayer Settings");
local Uk = game:GetService("Players");
local Pk = game:GetService("UserInputService");
local Ck = game:GetService("RunService");
local tk = Uk.LocalPlayer;
local Qk = false;
local hk = 50;
local dk;
local wk = {
		f = 0,
		b = 0,
		l = 0,
		r = 0,
	};
local ak, zk;
local function Ik()
	local function o()
		local o = tk.Character;
		if not o then
			return;
		end;
		local F = o:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid");
		if not F then
			return;
		end;
		local J = F.MoveDirection;
		wk.f = 0;
		wk.b = 0;
		wk.l = 0;
		wk.r = 0;
		if J.Z < -0.1 then
			wk.f = 1;
		elseif J.Z > .1 then
			wk.b = 1;
		end;
		if J.X < -0.1 then
			wk.l = 1;
		elseif J.X > .1 then
			wk.r = 1;
		end;
	end;
	local F;
	F = Ck.Heartbeat:Connect(function()
			if Qk then
				o();
			else
				if F then
					F:Disconnect();
				end;
			end;
		end);
end;
local function xk(o)
	Qk = o;
	if Qk then
		if not tk.Character then
			return;
		end;
		local o = tk.Character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid");
		local F;
		if tk.Character:FindFirstChild("Torso") then
			F = tk.Character.Torso;
		else
			F = tk.Character.UpperTorso;
		end;
		if not o or not F then
			return;
		end;
		for o, F in ipairs(tk.Character:GetDescendants()) do
			if F:IsA("BasePart") then
				F.CanCollide = false;
				F.Massless = true;
			end;
		end;
		local J;
		J = tk.Character.DescendantAdded:Connect(function(o)
				if Qk and o:IsA("BasePart") then
					o.CanCollide = false;
					o.Massless = true;
				end;
			end);
		ak = Instance.new("BodyGyro", F);
		ak.P = 90000.0;
		ak.maxTorque = Vector3.new(9000000000.0, 9000000000.0, 9000000000.0);
		ak.cframe = F.CFrame;
		zk = Instance.new("BodyVelocity", F);
		zk.velocity = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0);
		zk.maxForce = Vector3.new(9000000000.0, 9000000000.0, 9000000000.0);
		o.PlatformStand = true;
		Ik();
		dk = Ck.Heartbeat:Connect(function()
				if not Qk or not tk.Character then
					return;
				end;
				for o, F in ipairs(tk.Character:GetDescendants()) do
					if F:IsA("BasePart") and F.CanCollide then
						F.CanCollide = false;
					end;
				end;
				if wk.l + wk.r ~= 0 or wk.f + wk.b ~= 0 then
					zk.velocity = (workspace.CurrentCamera.CoordinateFrame.lookVector * (wk.f + wk.b) + (workspace.CurrentCamera.CoordinateFrame * (CFrame.new(wk.l + wk.r, (wk.f + wk.b) * .2, 0)).p - workspace.CurrentCamera.CoordinateFrame.p)) * hk;
				else
					zk.velocity = Vector3.new(0, 0, 0);
				end;
				ak.cframe = workspace.CurrentCamera.CoordinateFrame;
			end);
	else
		if dk then
			dk:Disconnect();
			dk = nil;
		end;
		if tk.Character then
			local o = tk.Character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Humanoid");
			if o then
				o.PlatformStand = false;
			end;
			for o, F in ipairs(tk.Character:GetDescendants()) do
				if F:IsA("BasePart") then
					F.CanCollide = true;
					F.Massless = false;
				end;
			end;
			if ak then
				ak:Destroy();
			end;
			if zk then
				zk:Destroy();
			end;
		end;
		wk = {
				f = 0,
				b = 0,
				l = 0,
				r = 0,
			};
	end;
end;
local function bk(o)
	hk = o;
end;
tk.CharacterAdded:Connect(function(o)
	wait(1);
	if Qk then
		xk(false);
		wait(.1);
		xk(true);
	end;
end);
I.Combat:AddToggle({ Name = "Enable Fly", Default = false, Callback = function(o)
		xk(o);
	end });
I.Combat:AddSlider({
	Name = "Speed Fly Mode",
	Min = 10,
	Max = 200,
	Default = 50,
	Callback = function(o)
		bk(o);
	end,
});
I.Combat:AddToggle({ Name = "Dash No Cooldown", Default = false, Callback = function(o)
		(getgenv()).DodgeNoCD = o;
	end });
local function Lk()
	local o = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:WaitForChild("Dodge");
	for F, J in next, getgc() do
		if typeof(J) == "function" then
			local F = getfenv(J);
			if F.script == o then
				for o, F in next, getupvalues(J) do
					if tostring(F) == "0.4" then
						setupvalue(J, o, 0);
					end;
				end;
			end;
		end;
	end;
end;

I.Misc:AddButton({ Name = "Hop Server", Description = "", Callback = function()
		task.spawn(function()
			local o = game:GetService("HttpService");
			local F = game:GetService("TeleportService");
			local J = game.PlaceId;
			local D = game:GetService("Players");
			local G, m = pcall(function()
					local F = "https://games.roblox.com/v1/games/" .. (J .. "/servers/Public?sortOrder=Asc&limit=100");
					local D = game:HttpGet(F);
					return (o:JSONDecode(D)).data;
				end);
			if G and m then
				local o;
				for F, J in pairs(m) do
					if J.playing < J.maxPlayers then
						o = J.id;
					end;
				end;
				if o then
					pcall(function()
						F:TeleportToPlaceInstance(J, o, D.LocalPlayer);
					end);
				end;
			end;
		end);
	end });
I.Misc:AddButton({ Name = "Hop to Lowest Players", Description = "", Callback = function()
		local o = game:GetService("HttpService");
		local F = game:GetService("TeleportService");
		local J = "https://games.roblox.com/v1/games/";
		local D = game.PlaceId;
		local G = J .. (D .. "/servers/Public?sortOrder=Asc&limit=100");
		function ListServers(F)
			local J = game:HttpGet(G .. (F and "&cursor=" .. F or ""));
			return o:JSONDecode(J);
		end;
		local m, X;
		repeat
			local o = ListServers(X);
			m = o.data[1];
			X = o.nextPageCursor;
		until m;
		F:TeleportToPlaceInstance(D, m.id, Bk);
	end });
I.Misc:AddButton({ Name = "Hop to Lowest Pings Server", Description = "", Callback = function()
		local o = game:GetService("HttpService");
		local F = game:GetService("TeleportService");
		local J = game:GetService("Stats");
		local function D(F, J)
			local D = string.format("https://games.roblox.com/v1/games/%d/servers/Public?limit=%d", F, J);
			local G, m = pcall(function()
					return o:JSONDecode(game:HttpGet(D));
				end);
			if G and (m and m.data) then
				return m.data;
			end;
			return nil;
		end;
		local G = game.PlaceId;
		local m = 100;
		local X = D(G, m);
		if not X then
			return;
		end;
		local V = X[1];
		for o, F in pairs(X) do
			if F.ping < V.ping and F.maxPlayers > F.playing then
				V = F;
			end;
		end;
		local j = .5;
		task.wait(j);
		local Y = 100;
		local B = J.Network.ServerStatsItem;
		local r = B["Data Ping"]:GetValueString();
		local A = tonumber(r:match("(%d+)"));
		if A >= Y then
			F:TeleportToPlaceInstance(G, V.id);
		else
 
		end;
	end });

rtxM = I.Misc:AddToggle({
		Name = "Turn on RTX Mode",
		Description = "",
		Default = false,
		Callback = function(o)
			_G.RTXMode = o;
			local F = game.Lighting;
			local J = Instance.new("ColorCorrectionEffect", F);
			local D = Instance.new("ColorCorrectionEffect", F);
			OldAmbient = F.Ambient;
			OldBrightness = F.Brightness;
			OldColorShift_Top = F.ColorShift_Top;
			OldBrightnessc = J.Brightness;
			OldContrastc = J.Contrast;
			OldTintColorc = J.TintColor;
			OldTintColore = D.TintColor;
			if not _G.RTXMode then
				return;
			end;
			while _G.RTXMode do
				wait();
				F.Ambient = Color3.fromRGB(33, 33, 33);
				F.Brightness = .3;
				J.Brightness = .176;
				J.Contrast = .39;
				J.TintColor = Color3.fromRGB(217, 145, 57);
				game.Lighting.FogEnd = 999;
				if not Bk.Character.HumanoidRootPart:FindFirstChild("PointLight") then
					local o = Instance.new("PointLight");
					o.Parent = Bk.Character.HumanoidRootPart;
					o.Range = 15;
					o.Color = Color3.fromRGB(217, 145, 57);
				end;
				if not _G.RTXMode then
					F.Ambient = OldAmbient;
					F.Brightness = OldBrightness;
					F.ColorShift_Top = OldColorShift_Top;
					J.Contrast = OldContrastc;
					J.Brightness = OldBrightnessc;
					J.TintColor = OldTintColorc;
					D.TintColor = OldTintColore;
					game.Lighting.FogEnd = 2500;
					(Bk.Character.HumanoidRootPart:FindFirstChild("PointLight")):Destroy();
				end;
			end;
		end,
	});

I.Misc:AddButton({ Name = "Rain Fruits (Client)", Description = "", Callback = function()

			if F.Fruit:FindFirstChild("AnimationController") then
				((F.Fruit:FindFirstChild("AnimationController")):LoadAnimation(F.Fruit:FindFirstChild("Idle"))):Play();
			end;
			F.Handle.Touched:Connect(function(o)
				if o.Parent == Bk.Character then
					F.Parent = Bk.Backpack;
					Bk.Character.Humanoid:EquipTool(F);
				end;
			end);
		end;
	end });
