dayornight = I.Misc:AddToggle({
		Name = "Turn on Time",
		Description = "",
		Default = false,
		Callback = function(o)
			_G.daylightN = o;
		end,
	});
task.spawn(function()
	while task.wait() do
		if _G.daylightN then
			if _G.SelectDN == "Day" then
				Lighting.ClockTime = 12;
			elseif _G.SelectDN == "Night" then
				Lighting.ClockTime = 0;
			end;
		end;
	end;
end);
walkWater = I.Misc:AddToggle({
		Name = "Turn on Walk on Water",
		Description = "",
		Default = true,
		Callback = function(o)
			_G.WalkWater_Part = o;
			if _G.WalkWater_Part then
				(game:GetService("Workspace")).Map["WaterBase-Plane"].Size = Vector3.new(1000, 112, 1000);
			else
				(game:GetService("Workspace")).Map["WaterBase-Plane"].Size = Vector3.new(1000, 80, 1000);
			end;
		end,
	});
iceWalk = I.Misc:AddToggle({
		Name = "Turn on Ice Walk",
		Description = "",
		Default = false,
		Callback = function(o)
			_G.WalkWater = o;
		end,
	});
spawn(function()
	while task.wait() do
		if _G.WalkWater then
			pcall(function()
				if Bk.Character and Bk.Character:FindFirstChild("LeftFoot") then
					local o = ek.Assets.Models.IceSpikes4:Clone();
					o.Parent = workspace;
					o.Size = Vector3.new(3 + math.random(10, 12), 1.7, 3 + math.random(10, 12));
					o.Color = Color3.fromRGB(128, 187, 219);
					o.CFrame = CFrame.new(Bk.Character.Head.Position.X, -3.8, Bk.Character.Head.Position.Z) * CFrame.Angles((math.random() - .5) * .06, math.random() * 7, (math.random() - .5) * .07);
					local F = {};
					F.Size = Vector3.new(0, .3, 0);
					local J = TW:Create(o, TweenInfo.new(2, Enum.EasingStyle.Quad, Enum.EasingDirection.In), F);
					J.Completed:Connect(function()
						o:Destroy();
					end);
					J:Play();
				end;
			end);
		end;
	end;
end);
local Ok = game.Players.LocalPlayer;
local function yk(o)
	if not o then
		return false;
	end;
	local F = o:FindFirstChild("Humanoid");
	return F and F.Health > 0;
end;
local function Hk(o, F)
	local J = (game:GetService("Workspace")).Enemies:GetChildren();
	local D = (game:GetService("Players")):GetPlayers();
	local G = {};
	local m = (o:GetPivot()).Position;
	for o, J in ipairs(J) do
		local D = J:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart");
		if D and yk(J) then
			local o = (D.Position - m).Magnitude;
			if o <= F then
				table.insert(G, J);
			end;
		end;
	end;
	for o, J in ipairs(D) do
		if J ~= Ok and J.Character then
			local o = J.Character:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart");
			if o and yk(J.Character) then
				local D = (o.Position - m).Magnitude;
				if D <= F then
					table.insert(G, J.Character);
				end;
			end;
		end;
	end;
	return G;
end;
function AttackNoCoolDown()
	local o = (game:GetService("Players")).LocalPlayer;
	local F = o.Character;
	if not F then
		return;
	end;
	local J = nil;
	for o, F in ipairs(F:GetChildren()) do
		if F:IsA("Tool") then
			J = F;
			break;
		end;
	end;
	if not J then
		return;
	end;
	local D = Hk(F, 60);
	if #D == 0 then
		return;
	end;
	local G = game:GetService("ReplicatedStorage");
	local m = G:FindFirstChild("Modules");
	if not m then
		return;
	end;
	local X = ((G:WaitForChild("Modules")):WaitForChild("Net")):WaitForChild("RE/RegisterAttack");
	local V = ((G:WaitForChild("Modules")):WaitForChild("Net")):WaitForChild("RE/RegisterHit");
	if not X or not V then
		return;
	end;
	local j, Y = {}, nil;
	for o, F in ipairs(D) do
		if not F:GetAttribute("IsBoat") then
			local o = {
					"RightLowerArm",
					"RightUpperArm",
					"LeftLowerArm",
					"LeftUpperArm",
					"RightHand",
					"LeftHand",
				};
			local J = F:FindFirstChild(o[math.random(#o)]) or F.PrimaryPart;
			if J then
				table.insert(j, { F, J });
				Y = J;
			end;
		end;
	end;
	if not Y then
		return;
	end;
	X:FireServer(0);
	local B = o:FindFirstChild("PlayerScripts");
	if not B then
		return;
	end;
	local r = B:FindFirstChildOfClass("LocalScript");
	while not r do
		B.ChildAdded:Wait();
		r = B:FindFirstChildOfClass("LocalScript");
	end;
	local A;
	if getsenv then
		local o, F = pcall(getsenv, r);
		if o and F then
			A = F._G.SendHitsToServer;
		end;
	end;
	local g, l = pcall(function()
			return (require(m.Flags)).COMBAT_REMOTE_THREAD or false;
		end);
	if g and (l and A) then
		A(Y, j);
	elseif g and not l then
		V:FireServer(Y, j);
	end;
end;
CameraShakerR = require(game.ReplicatedStorage.Util.CameraShaker);
CameraShakerR:Stop();
get_Monster = function()
		for o, F in pairs(workspace.Enemies:GetChildren()) do
			local J = F:FindFirstChild("UpperTorso") or F:FindFirstChild("Head");
			if F:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart", true) and J then
				if (F.Head.Position - Bk.Character.HumanoidRootPart.Position).Magnitude <= 50 then
					return true, J.Position;
				end;
			end;
		end;
		for o, F in pairs(workspace.SeaBeasts:GetChildren()) do
			if F:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart") and (F:FindFirstChild("Health") and F.Health.Value > 0) then
				return true, F.HumanoidRootPart.Position;
			end;
		end;
		for o, F in pairs(workspace.Enemies:GetChildren()) do
			if F:FindFirstChild("Health") and (F.Health.Value > 0 and F:FindFirstChild("VehicleSeat")) then
				return true, F.Engine.Position;
			end;
		end;
	end;
Actived = function()
		local o = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Tool");
		for o, F in next, getconnections(o.Activated) do
			if typeof(F.Function) == "function" then
				getupvalues(F.Function);
			end;
		end;
	end;
task.spawn(function()
	RunSer.Heartbeat:Connect(function()
		pcall(function()
			if not _G.Seriality then
				return;
			end;
			AttackNoCoolDown();
			local o = game.Players.LocalPlayer.Character:FindFirstChildOfClass("Tool");
			local F = o.ToolTip;
			local J, D = get_Monster();
			if F == "Blox Fruit" then
				if J then
					local F = o:FindFirstChild("LeftClickRemote");
					if F then
						Actived();
						F:FireServer(Vector3.new(.01, -500, .01), 1, true);
						F:FireServer(false);
					end;
				end;
			end;
		end);
	end);
end);
local Tk = {};
local Ek = {};
local fk = {};
local uk = game;
local Rk = uk:GetService("Players");
local ck = uk:GetService("RunService");
local kk = uk:GetService("ReplicatedStorage");
local nk = uk:GetService("Workspace");
local Mk = Rk.LocalPlayer;
local pk = Mk.Character or Mk.CharacterAdded:Wait();
local function Kk(o, F)
	local J, D = pcall(function()
			return o:WaitForChild(F);
		end);
	return D;
end;
local oa = Kk(nk, "Enemies");
local Fa = Kk(nk, "Characters");
local Ja = Kk(kk, "Modules");
local Da = Kk(Ja, "Net");
Tk.Rate = 2e-009;
Tk.Enabled = true;
function Tk.IsAlive(o)
	local F = o:FindFirstChild("Humanoid");
	if F and F.Health > 0 then
		return true;
	end;
	return false;
end;
function Tk.GetNearbyTargets(o, F)
	local J = (o:GetPivot()).Position;
	local D = {};
	local G = F:GetChildren();
	for o = 1, #G, 1 do
		local F = G[o];
		local m = F:FindFirstChild("Humanoid");
		local X = F:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart");
		if m and (X and m.Health > 0) then
			local o = (X.Position - J).Magnitude;
			if o <= 60 then
				table.insert(D, F);
			end;
		end;
	end;
	return D;
end;
function Tk.GetTargetParts(o)
	local F = {};
	local J = #o;
	for J = 1, J, 1 do
		local D = o[J];
		local G = D:FindFirstChild("Head") or D.PrimaryPart;
		if G then
			table.insert(F, { D, G });
		end;
	end;
	return F;
end;
function Tk.GetAllTargets(o)
	local F = Tk.GetNearbyTargets(o, oa);
	local J = Tk.GetNearbyTargets(o, Fa);
	local D = {};
	for o = 1, #F, 1 do
		table.insert(D, F[o]);
	end;
	for o = 1, #J, 1 do
		table.insert(D, J[o]);
	end;
	return D;
end;
function Tk.ExecuteFastAttack()
	local o = Mk.Character;
	if not o then
		return;
	end;
	local F = o:FindFirstChildOfClass("Tool");
	if not F then
		return;
	end;
	local J = Tk.GetAllTargets(o);
	if #J < 1 then
		return;
	end;
	local D = Tk.GetTargetParts(J);
	if #D < 1 then
		return;
	end;
	local G = Da["RE/RegisterAttack"];
	local m = Da["RE/RegisterHit"];
	G:FireServer(Tk.Rate);
	local X = D[1][2];
	m:FireServer(X, D);
end;
local Ga;
local ma;
local function Xa()
	local o = {
			kk.Util,
			kk.Common,
			kk.Remotes,
			kk.Assets,
			kk.FX,
		};
	for o, F in ipairs(o) do
		local J = F:GetChildren();
		for o, F in ipairs(J) do
			if F:IsA("RemoteEvent") and F:GetAttribute("Id") then
				Ga = F;
				ma = F:GetAttribute("Id");
			end;
		end;
		F.ChildAdded:Connect(function(o)
			if o:IsA("RemoteEvent") and o:GetAttribute("Id") then
				Ga = o;
				ma = o:GetAttribute("Id");
			end;
		end);
	end;
end;
Xa();
function Ek.Execute()
	local o = Mk.Character;
	if not o then
		return;
	end;
	local F = o:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart");
	if not F then
		return;
	end;
	local J = {};
	local function D(D)
		local G = D:GetChildren();
		for D = 1, #G, 1 do
			local m = G[D];
			local X = m:FindFirstChild("Humanoid");
			local V = m:FindFirstChild("HumanoidRootPart");
			if X and (V and (X.Health > 0 and m ~= o)) then
				local o = (V.Position - F.Position).Magnitude;
				if o <= 60 then
					local o = m:GetChildren();
					for o, F in ipairs(o) do
						if F:IsA("BasePart") then
							table.insert(J, { m, F });
						end;
					end;
				end;
			end;
		end;
	end;
	D(oa);
	D(Fa);
	local G = o:FindFirstChildOfClass("Tool");
	if #J > 0 and (G and (G:GetAttribute("WeaponType") == "Melee" or G:GetAttribute("WeaponType") == "Sword")) then
		local o = Ja.Net.seed:InvokeServer();
		local F = Da["RE/RegisterAttack"];
		local D = Da["RE/RegisterHit"];
		F:FireServer();
		local G = J[1][1]:FindFirstChild("Head");
		if not G then
			return;
		end;
		D:FireServer(G, J, {});
		if Ga then
			local F = "RE/RegisterHit";
			local D = math.floor((nk:GetServerTimeNow() / 10) % 10) + 1;
			local m = string.gsub(F, ".", function(o)
					return string.char(bit32.bxor(string.byte(o), D));
				end);
			local X = bit32.bxor(ma + 909090, o * 2);
			(cloneref(Ga)):FireServer(m, X, G, J);
		end;
	end;
end;
local function Va()
	local o = require(kk.Util.CameraShaker);
	o:Stop();
end;
local function ja()
	task.spawn(function()
		while task.wait(Tk.Rate) do
			Tk.ExecuteFastAttack();
		end;
	end);
	ck.Heartbeat:Connect(function()
		pcall(Ek.Execute);
	end);
end;
ja();
